Qiu Shuyuan During the Cession of Taiwan

— Zheng Yimei

The cession of Taiwan to Japan is a major page in the history of national humiliation. The land is in eastern Fujian, comprising twenty-nine islands. It originally belonged to our country's territory. During the late Ming Dynasty, it was occupied by the Dutch. Zheng Chenggong expelled the Dutch and took it over. After the fall of the Zheng family, it reverted to the Qing Dynasty. Unexpectedly, after the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95, we lost the war and the land, and the Treaty of Shimonoseki stipulated the cession of Taiwan. However, the people of Taiwan had been deeply influenced by our country's culture and civilization. Patriots rose up to resist the Japanese, and Qiu Shuyuan was their leader. Qiu Shuyuan, whose given name was Wei Xuan, was originally from Haicheng, Fujian.

His ancestors moved to Taiwan, and he settled there. His family assets were in the millions. He was known for his generosity at the time. When the Qing court ceded Taiwan, Shuyuan repeatedly telegraphed to argue against it. He even wrote a memorial in blood. The Qing court did not listen. Shuyuan was extremely indignant and said, "The court has abandoned the land and people of Taiwan. The people of Taiwan must find a way to extricate themselves." He contributed his family wealth to support the army and organized the Republic of Formosa, electing Tang Jingsong and Liu Yongfu as president and vice president, respectively. Later, the provincial garrison troops mutinied, burning the government office and looting the treasury. The rebellion failed. Shuyuan could not bear to be under Japanese citizenship. Therefore, he went to Guangdong. He also lived in Singapore, calling himself the "Retired Gentleman of Xingzhou." He founded the Tiannan Newspaper. Later, he built a house in his old residence in Haicheng to take care of his parents. He lectured at the Hanshan and Dongshan Academies in Chaozhou. He also founded the Lingdong Tongwen Academy. During the Xinhai Revolution, Shuyuan briefly served as Minister of Education. He was also elected as a representative of Guangdong. After the unification of the North and South, he was elected as a senator. He died of illness shortly after. It was March 25th of the first year of the Republic. His life's works include "Shuyuan's Trivial Talks" in eight volumes, followed by "Occasional Remnants of Gengyin" and "Poems of Ren Chen." Among them are poems harmonizing with ancient themes, such as "Bo Yi": "Not meeting the Yellow Emperor and Shennong, but the Xia Dynasty. The shadows of brothers alone in the universe. Subtle words want to be sent by the clear wind. Tang and Wu have learned from Shun and Yao since ancient times." "Su Wu": "Ten thousand miles of mountains and passes, the moonlight is fading. Herding rams in the snowy cave, enduring the desolate cold. Returning, I do not see my living wife. I should regret marrying a woman in the land of the Huns." "Yang Xiong": "It's not that writing is not important for thousands of years. It turns out to praise the new dynasty with writing. If you want to ask the rulers in the Nine Springs, how can this hatred be dispelled?" They are truly valuable works. Reading his poems allows one to imagine the person. Thus, I record it as such.

World Briefs

A Couple Married for Seventy-Four Years: In Wainfleet, Lincolnshire, England, there is an elderly man named William Walker who has been married for seventy-four years. This is considered the longest marriage record in England. He is ninety-four years old this year, and his wife is ninety-three years old. They have a son who is seventy years old. This family of elders lives a very happy life, which is truly enviable. According to Mr. Walker, "When we got married, all we had was two pounds in cash. The furniture in the house consisted of only a bed, a table, and a few chairs. At that time, I was helping people work in the fields, earning two shillings a day. But we tried our best to save and put aside a little money. So now we can live in our own house, and we have some other property. We also have some savings in the bank." Regarding the way to a loving marriage, Mrs. Walker has a good recipe that can be introduced to women all over the world. Mrs. Walker said, "Always make sure your husband eats well, and no matter what, let him do what he wants to do. There is no need to argue with him. This is the only way to keep him calm, and this is very important in married life."

An Overview of Ma Zhanshan's Troop Training

— Rui Yucheng

General Ma Zhanshan's troops are all strong men in their prime. They rise at 5:00 AM and sleep at 8:00 PM. During the day, they undergo five training sessions and three lectures. There is also an emergency assembly at midnight. Soldiers are often awakened from deep sleep by the sound of sirens. They immediately jump up and put on their full gear in the dark. They also have to fold their bedding neatly. Then, they grope for their guns in the armory. They then line up on the parade ground. The time elapsed is only five minutes. If their clothes are not neat, their bedding is messy, or they grab the wrong gun, they will be punished.

The most unbearable things are the midnight assembly in winter and the midday drill in summer. After the former assembly, they start running for thirty minutes. The soldiers are sweating profusely. Suddenly, they stand still for a lecture, which also lasts for twenty to thirty minutes. At that time, the sweat on the soldiers' clothes is immediately frozen into ice by the cold wind during the lecture. When they change clothes after the dismissal, the skin on their chest and back has been scraped off by the ice. This happens every day. The latter occurs in the hot summer. They have a drill every day at noon. Often, after the drill, the soldiers' clothes, which are originally gray, are covered with a layer of white frost, which is formed by the condensation of sweat.

There are also regulations for meals. Each person can only eat twelve taels of corn rice per meal. As for vegetables, a company shares a pot of green vegetables, with only four taels of soybean oil added. Other breakfast side dishes are either two pieces of radish per person or one pickled green vegetable per person.

There is also a kind of field training. Often, they go out for several months before returning. No dry food is prepared. They eat wherever they go.

Soldiers always wear military uniforms and are not allowed to wear casual clothes. They are not allowed to wear rings or other extravagant items. The most forbidden things are prostitution and gambling. Therefore, they must stay in camp every night. If they do not answer the roll call, they will be severely punished.

In summary, although it is a simple overview, it also shows the spirit of General Ma's troop training. Imagine soldiers who have undergone such rigorous training. How can they not be brave and strong? I hope that all the troops in our country are like this. Then, how can we have the fear of national destruction?

Parental Education

— Sun Choucheng

The China Philanthropic Association for Children aims to assist in the happiness of children. It is jointly organized by Chinese and American educators. The chairman is Minister Kong Xiangxi. There are two vice-chairmen: Dr. Luo Yunyan and Mrs. Guo Bingwen. Other executive committee members are enthusiastic philanthropists from both China and the United States, half men and half women, regardless of nationality and gender. They are all very diligent in their association affairs. The general manager, Wu Weide, is shrewd and capable, so the association's affairs are thriving. The other day, the association held a meeting and invited Professor Chen Heqin, the current director of the Chinese Education Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council and the editor-in-chief of the Children's Education Monthly, to give a lecture. Choucheng went to participate. Because what Mr. Chen said about children's education starts with parental education, it is indeed a fundamental solution. We who are over forty years old and have children must adopt this kind of proposition. I dare not keep it to myself. Therefore, I have extracted the main points I heard that day as follows.

Children are born from parents. If you want to talk about children's education, you should first pay attention to father-child training. Parental education is the prerequisite for children's training. The mistakes that parents make with children are due to viewing children as their own property, their own successors. Because they are not yet adults, they are called "little people." They do not recognize that they have knowledge. Therefore, problems arise between children and parents, thinking that parents are always right, and their mistakes must be in the children. This is why our country has the saying "There are no parents in the world who are wrong." Parents treat their children according to their own joys and sorrows. When happy, they play with the children, making them laugh. When unhappy, they beat and scold the children, forcing them to cry. Even when husband and wife are at odds, they vent their anger on the children, not knowing that children are rich in imitation. They pay close attention to every move of their parents. Therefore, as parents, they should be careful about children's education everywhere. If there is any discord between husband and wife, even if they want to quarrel, they should avoid the children's presence. Otherwise, bad impressions will enter the children's minds, which is very inappropriate. Also, children are naturally lively and naturally active. In our country's old customs, children are often forbidden to play, wanting to cultivate a gentle and refined attitude, which is completely contrary to educational principles. The best thing for parents to do is to be bystanders in all of the children's actions, without always assuming that children's knowledge is incomplete, wanting to supervise and help with their own ideas, and interfering horizontally. Children have the psychology of children and should follow their psychology to develop the habit of doing things from an early age. This is what parents should pay attention to.

Moral Education and Aesthetic Education (Part 2)

— Fang Jiangshui

However, how to cultivate the spirit is difficult to say. In the past, the Englishman Spencer wrote "Knowable" and "Unknowable." At the beginning of our lives, we are ignorant.

Coming, I do not know where I came from. After I die, the spirit is annihilated, and I do not know where I am going. This is the mystery of life and cannot be known.

As the saying goes, humans are the most intelligent of all things, which means that humans can know the intelligence of all things. What we do not know may be more intelligent than humans, so I also have things I know and do not know about how to cultivate personality and I do not dare to be confident.

The establishment of every theory has its own outline. Therefore, Christianity has the Creed, Islam has the Creed, and Taoism and Buddhism have the Creed. The cultivation of the spirit also has a creed. Although opinions vary, the creeds are different. It is okay to say wisdom, benevolence, and courage. It is also okay to say love, affection, and sincerity. I have thought about this many times. Now, please let me elaborate on it and discuss it with you. There are five creeds.

First, be ambitious. As the saying goes, all evils are born of short-sightedness. Therefore, those who want to accomplish great things cannot be constrained by trivial matters. Their minds should be broad, and their vision should be far-sighted. Zigong said, "The wise discuss the big things, and the unworthy know the small things." This is the difference between great men and small men.

Second, be transcendent and open-minded. "Transcendent" means detached, and "open-minded" means magnanimous. This should be the case with fame and fortune. The ancients said that before the Three Dynasties, people were afraid of fame. Why should one's own name be desired to be passed down forever? Even to the point of deliberately distorting and fabricating to gain fame and reputation. However, what do we know about the name after death? Even if there are books, they may be discarded. What can we do? I only know that the spirit has a place to be entrusted. Do not be honored by gaining fame, and do not be worried about losing fame. Just listen to it. As for the pursuit of material things, insatiable greed is even more meaningless. The unrest in society is caused by this. People's desires are hard to fill. A lifetime of energy is wasted on this. How pitiful! It is enough to have a decent life. What is the benefit of excessive pursuit?

Third, be diligent and hard-working. Whether one is a saint, a sage, a hero, or a great man, or even a villain, a traitor, or a rebellious son, nothing can be achieved without diligence and hard work. As the saying goes, "Excellence comes from diligence." If you are not diligent in walking, it is difficult to reach your destination. If you are not diligent in eating and drinking, you will not be full all day. Shouldn't we encourage each other?

Fourth, be honest and sincere. People who are honest and do not deceive can gain the trust of society. This is the way to be sincere to others. Work hard and study diligently. You can achieve success. This is the way to be sincere to yourself. The ancients said, "Where sincerity reaches, even metal and stone will be opened." Only with sincerity can all undertakings be accomplished.

Fifth, be benevolent and kind. When people come into contact with each other, love arises. Only when people love each other can there be peace. Confucius said, "The benevolent love people." He also said, "Love all people and be close to the benevolent." Therefore, the words "benevolence and kindness" are the ropes that maintain society. This should be the case with people, and it should also be the case with things, so as to avoid the occurrence of cruel and inhumane events.

The above five are extremely ordinary and extremely common. Everyone can achieve them, and none can be missing. Like the five grains to human life, they are born if they are obtained and die if they are abandoned. If people can pay attention to cultivating themselves in this regard, then noble thoughts, great spirit, and pure personality can be established. With such thoughts, spirit, and personality, whether one is writing articles, poems, books, or paintings, or extending it to everything else, one can reach the realm of perfection. Isn't this just being a simple artist? Therefore, I say that moral education is also the foundation of education. (Moved to help with disaster relief)

War! (Part 2)

— Wang Weibin

"At that time, I was under Wang Zhiping, and we were ordered to go to Huangdu."

"Were you afraid?" I asked, deliberately.

"Tch! What's there to be afraid of?"

"What were your thoughts at the time?"

"No thoughts."

"No, because I want to study the psychology of soldiers, please think about what you felt at the time, what kind of expectations did you have?" I pressed him closely.

He thought for a while and replied, "I felt like I was going to a strange place, and if there was a possibility of contact, it would be meaningful. As for what I expected, I felt like I was about to change my position."

"Did you think about the danger of separation from your comrades nearby?"

"No, we seemed to be full of enthusiasm, hoping to see some victory soon. We were very relaxed in the trenches not far from the station, playing chess, playing mahjong, thick bottles of foreign wine, canned cigarettes and food, we enjoyed ourselves to the fullest. At that time, everything was much more equal than usual except for military orders."

He continued, "At that time, we played mahjong, using whole pieces of cooked ham, cutting them with knives and eating them, listening to the sound of guns and cannons outside. If it got close, we could play another round. Scouts often reported news from the trenches, the telephone rang constantly, and the sound of guns was close. 'Let's go out and "deal with it"!' So we closed the mahjong tiles, grabbed our weapons, and went to "deal with it." I remember that on August 17, the Soviet army rushed into Huangdu Station, but this time it was a victory. The two regimental commanders, Wang and Li Mingcheng (the old foreigner from Henan), bravely sacrificed themselves for the country while charging forward!"

It can be seen that such Chinese troops did not have the idea of life and death when facing the enemy. That Chinese war did not frighten foreigners, let alone the Japanese devils. We used five people to fight to the death against one Japanese person. When the Japanese were dead, half of the Chinese were still left, and 200 million compatriots were left to revitalize China.

War! is the only way out for the Chinese nation to survive today!

Finance: Interest Rates Slightly Higher, Interbank Lending Still Loose

The market is very quiet during the bank closures.

Market Overview: In the past two days, due to the bank closures of the Bank of China, although Chinese merchants were operating as usual, it was also relatively quiet. However, the current money supply has loosened, and the impact on various relationships has largely returned to normal. However, the year-end settlement of funds by the silver and money industry is quite difficult, and the return of accounts by customers is particularly slow. The financial crisis is more difficult than any other year-end.

Interest Rate Prices (Foreign Interest Rate): The early morning interest rate was 7 qian 2 fen 2 li 6 hao 2 hu and a half. The noon interest rate was 7 qian 2 fen 3 li 1 hao 2 hu and a half, which seemed to be half a li better than the previous day. (Silver Interest Rate): Both the morning and noon markets were 8 fen, which was the same as the previous day. The situation was quite weak, and it has probably returned to the old situation.

Subsidiary Currency Market: The Jiangnan small silver dollar early morning was still 6 qian 5 fen 4 li. The noon market was reduced by 1 li, calculated as 6 qian 5 fen 3 li. The transaction volume in the early morning was 3,000 jiao, and in the noon market, it was 2,500 jiao. The Guangdong small silver dollar early morning was 6 qian 5 fen 7 li and a half. The noon market was 6 qian 5 fen 8 li, which was also 1 li lower than the previous day. The transaction volume in the early morning was 95,000 jiao, and in the noon market, it was 40,000 jiao. Copper coins were reduced by 2,500 wen to 364,000 wen.

Inflow and Outflow of Silver Dollars (Silver Funds): Yesterday, foreign merchants' banks were still closed. On the Chinese merchants' side, in addition to the Bund holiday, although there were receipts and deliveries, they were also sparse. Silver firms and money changers received and delivered more than 45 million yuan. The receipts and deliveries of head-scratching money are unknown. The amount of remittances from various routes was more than 200,000 yuan. (Foreign Funds): The early morning transaction volume of remittances and drafts was 695,000 yuan, and banknotes were 45,000 yuan. The noon market transaction volume of remittances and drafts was 1,285,000 yuan, and banknotes were 70,000 yuan. Yarn and Cotton: The Yarn Market Remains Dull

The yarn market was weak in the morning and strong at noon, with a slightly softer trend. This is because the financial situation is extremely tight, the actual demand has not been smooth, and the year-end is approaching, so the various gangs have no excitement, so the market situation is still dull. Recent Cotton Prices Surge by More Than Half a Liang

The cotton market is firm. This month, due to the Ningbo gang receiving goods, shipping them to Yongdi for delivery, the standard price suddenly rose by 5.5 qian, and the distant months were also lifted. However, the actual sales factories did not ask about it, because foreign cotton is cheap, so there is no need to buy local cotton again. However, the Han gang and the inland gangs have a very strong bullish mentality and have been holding on tightly from beginning to end, so it is difficult to be bearish for the time being.

The Han Standard Yong Gang Received Goods This Month: The exchange Han Standard opened in the morning. The US and Indian cotton markets were closed for Christmas. The market atmosphere in the market was average. There was no rise or fall in each month. In the afternoon, the current month was received by the Yong gang, rising by 5.5 qian alone, and the distant month rose by 1 qian. The total transaction volume for the day was 71,600 dan. It was found that Yudai sold 1,000 dan, Yichang sold 2,500 dan, Yuandai sold 2,200 dan, Shenchang sold 2,600 dan, Hengde sold 2,400 dan, and Rongxing sold 1,400 dan. Tianlong bought 4,400 dan, Changfeng bought 1,100 dan, Yiyu bought 1,200 dan, Jifeng bought 1,400 dan, and Gongtai bought 2,000 dan. The closing prices of the Han standard are listed on the left.

Spot Cotton Arrivals and Sales Are Both Quiet: There were no spot cotton transactions at all, and the source of supply was also cut off.

US Cotton is Expected to Turn Around After the New Year

A telegram from New York on the 24th reported on the cotton market in the past week. The cotton market was slightly firmer last week. Industry purchases were sufficient to absorb the South's selling. In terms of the overall market trend, everyone is uncertain as the New Year approaches, but there is an optimistic potential that the worst period has passed and a turnaround can be seen in the New Year. Moreover, the world's cotton inventory will be depleted due to limited sales in the past two years. However, public confidence must recover slowly after this unprecedented pressure. Moreover, the ultimate basis for cotton prices still depends on whether the cotton fields can be sharply reduced next season. At the same time, the legislative proposals in the winter parliament regarding agricultural relief have not been confirmed, and the new cotton planting season is approaching. The hoarding movement in the South may transform into softening.

Grain

Sparse Arrivals and Active Sales in the Hexia Rice Market

South Shanghai: Yesterday, the source of supply from various gangs suddenly became sluggish. About a dozen warehouses had weak inventories. The retail sales of urban and rural stores have been low for a long time, so they are still active, and transactions have become more concentrated. It is not easy for the thick Xinjing rice market to become firmer, because the year-end is approaching and the money supply is tight. There are fewer thin-rice arrivals every day. The price of slightly better-quality rice on this street has increased. Arrivals of foreign Dujian rice are sparse, and the appetite is turning active. The shape is挺秀. The accumulated inventory of the metamorphic yuan rice still has retail sales, which are still small. The alcohol appetite is not good, and the price has been reduced by another five fen.

Xinzha: 30 to 40 boats arrived. The market sales are旺 due to the bad weather. The buying interest from all parties is very strong. The prices of the two types of Xixin thin rice were raised by 1 jiao each. Foreign Dujian rice is sold as soon as it arrives, and the situation continues to be 挺. The Lingyu appetite of Tongjin rice is quiet and happy. The alcohol appetite of the metamorphic two yuan is寥寥, so the price has fallen by several fen. There are about 4,000 shi of Hexia 斛脚.

Various Gangs Continue to Sell Spot Small Rice

Price Increase of 1 Jiao

Yesterday, in the foreign rice market, the foreign banks were closed for the holidays, and the prices of returned goods were 喴高. Although there were no transactions in the market, people's hearts were looking forward to it. Yesterday was the delivery day for December 期粉. Sugar Market

Coarse Sand White Market Sentiment Turns Firm

Yesterday, there were no new dispatches from the sugar production areas to the sugar market. The clearing of accounts in the guild market was quiet due to it being Saturday. However, market sentiment was generally firm. Dutch sugar number 24 coarse sand white was bid at taels 9.65, then a few transactions were made at taels 9.6. There was a shortage of supply from producers. Dutch refined white sugar was taels 11.3, number 20 medium-grain white sugar taels 9.55, fine-ground white sugar taels 9.725 to 9.75, and Dutch red sugar number 8 taels 8.35. The market situation was generally stable and strong. Taikoo Sugar's China New Company offered over a hundred bags of CW mark at taels 11.65, B mark at taels 11.775 to 11.75, and DY mark bid at taels 11.7, with few takers. HX mark was at taels 11.55. Both buying and selling were slack, and the market seemed stable.

Piece Goods

The Nearing End of the Woolen Cloth Market

As the year draws to a close, the woolen cloth trade is gradually cooling down. The guild market situation is very quiet, as both buyers and sellers have mostly finished their accounting and wrapping up. In previous years, the woolen cloth business would have a major closing at the end of the lunar year. This year, the closing is earlier, mainly because most are following the Gregorian calendar. Also, the current market is unstable and financing is extremely tight. Therefore, although there are some sporadic transactions, most are cash on delivery or paid by check. There are very few transactions with promissory notes. The industry plans to settle outstanding accounts by the end of this month. However, for those with money houses, it will be settled by the end of January, according to the Chamber of Commerce notice. The accounts of tailors and seamstresses are unlikely to be collected by the end of January. Yesterday, Saturday, trading in the Tongyi Guild market was very sparse, and prices were falling rather than rising. The difference between open and hidden bids was significant, a rare occurrence in recent years. Yesterday, except for various plain and mixed-color broadcloths, other items such as straight tribute cloth, Walter cloth, fancy cloth, covert cloth, melton cloth, and raincoat fabric were all being sold at lower prices. Plain thick cloth and overcoat cloth showed a particularly sharp decline.

Metals: Approaching Peak Season But Sluggish Market Shows Signs of Fatigue

Yesterday, the metal market remained mediocre due to limited sales and weak demand from merchants. However, the arrival of goods was extensive, so the market showed signs of further weakness. Recently, there has been little hope for business improvement within the year for items such as plain galvanized iron, tinplate, pig lead, English steel plate, garden lead wire, and black iron sheet.

Black Iron Sheet: Two to Three Thousand Loads Arrived Yesterday

Black iron sheet, which was popular for a time, had a fresh arrival of two to three thousand loads in foreign warehouses yesterday, according to news. Most were 2'x6', while 3'x6' sheets were mostly 12 or 13 sheets per load. It is said that there was a limited amount of heavy-gauge colored sheets.

Coal: Large Shipment of Shanxi Coal to Arrive

Shanxi white coal prices have been steadily increasing due to limited supply, rising from 19 taels to over 21 taels per ton. Therefore, various local firms are procuring from Tianjin. It is now known that over seven thousand tons will be shipped. Yesterday, news from Tianjin stated that three thousand five hundred tons had been shipped and will arrive in Shanghai soon. If the goods arrive completely, the market may change slightly.

Local News

Jiang Zuobin, Chen Mingshu, etc.

Come to Shanghai to Urge Sun Ke

Sun Expresses Coming to Shanghai to Promote Unity Among Comrades

Hopes Hu, Wang, and Jiang Will All Go to Beijing to Preside

Since Sun Ke, Li Wenfan, and others suddenly left Beijing and came to Shanghai, the political atmosphere has become tense again. Yesterday, cars and horses crowded in front of Sun’s residence on Molihre Road. The conference specially dispatched envoys Jiang Zuobin, Chen Mingshu, Zou Lu, and others to come to Shanghai to urge him to return quickly. Sun himself issued a statement yesterday regarding his departure from Beijing and his future opinions. The news from yesterday is recorded below.

Jiang Zuobin Visits Sun After Sun Ke and others left Beijing,

the First Central Committee immediately held a discussion meeting that afternoon, deciding to first send Jiang Zuobin to Shanghai to explain. After arriving in Shanghai yesterday morning, Jiang visited Sun at 10:30 AM, talking for about an hour. Sun has not yet made a definitive statement on the issue of going to Beijing. Jiang returned to Beijing at 3:15 PM to report back.

Banquet for Li Jishen Li Jishen, a member of the Guangdong Committee remaining in Shanghai,

Li Zongren, Zhang Huichang, Chen Ce, Lin Yunga, Huang Shaoxiong, and others visited Sun’s residence yesterday morning one after another, asking in detail about the situation of the disputes. Sun prepared a meal at his residence, hosting a banquet for Li Jishen and others, which did not end until about 2 PM.

Telegraph to Hong Kong and Guangdong Sun Ke telegraphed

Hu Hanmin in Hong Kong, Chen Jitang and Xiao Focheng in Guangzhou, and others yesterday morning, reporting the details of the First Central Committee disputes.

Chen and Zou's Talk Chen Mingshu, acting head of the Executive Yuan, and Zou Lu, a member of the Central Committee,

were sent by the remaining members of the Central Committee in Beijing to come to Shanghai on the 12:30 PM train yesterday to urge Sun to return. They arrived here at 7:45 PM yesterday. The reporter went to meet them on the train. According to Zou Lu, the matter is not a major problem. He is only participating in the talks in a personal capacity. The various members of the Central Committee in Beijing have drafted a solution that can achieve a satisfactory resolution. The content of the solution cannot be disclosed yet, but it will likely be decided after they meet with Sun. The reporter also inquired with Chen, but Chen declined to express his opinion, answering roughly the same as Zou. Chen and Zou visited Sun once after arriving in Shanghai, leaving after a short talk. It is said that they will urge Sun to return again today.

Sun Ke Visits Wang Sun Zhesheng made an important statement regarding

his visit to Shanghai this time, expressing his attitude. After dinner, he personally visited Wang at Dr. Noehr's Hospital on Avenue Joffre, discussing the situation in Beijing and expressing concern for Wang’s illness.

Sun Ke's Statement Yesterday, through the introduction of a certain member of the Central Committee,

the reporter had an audience with Sun. Sun made a very candid statement, which is recorded below. (Reporter asked) What is the reason for your sudden departure from Beijing this time? Can you tell me? (Answer) My entry into Beijing this time was entirely based on the spirit of sincere unity and facing the national crisis together, hoping that the full meeting would bring an end to all previous party affairs and political disputes. Everyone should adopt the meaning of "dying yesterday and being born today," be open and honest, and unite anew, so that we can create a new life for the party and the country to seek a solution to the national crisis and satisfy the people's desires. However, since entering Beijing, I have been bedridden with illness for four or five days and have been unable to meet with my comrades to discuss matters in detail. However, the comrades I have met have all expressed the same feeling, and it is fortunate that the unification of the party and the country is now at hand, and the national vitality will arise from this. On the 24th of this month, I recovered from my illness. On that day, I was elected chairman of the first meeting. When the reform plan of the central political system was discussed, a certain member of the Central Committee, who is a big name, actually made many strange and bizarre remarks, doing his best to provoke discord. Fortunately, very few agreed, and the public ignored it. The second meeting continued yesterday, and I also attended. When the proposal of Comrade Yan Xishan and others to increase the allocation of 100,000 crack troops to defend Jinzhou was discussed, a certain member of the Central Committee again complained greatly, implicitly accusing the comrades from Guangdong who advocated punishing Zhang Xueliang of being traitors who sold out the country. This was not only seen in the remarks but also in the telegram sent to Zhang Xueliang. His malicious slander and intentional injury are certainly despicable. Moreover, at the First Central Committee meeting, which is the lifeline of the party and the country, how should those attending put aside their emotions and discuss matters openly? Yet, they regard their comrades as enemies and traitors. Is there any hope for the future of the party? Seeing this situation, I deeply feel that if such erroneous ideas in the party members are not corrected, there will never be any hope of unity. Therefore, after thinking it over again and again, the only option is to leave Beijing, regardless of causing another dispute within the party again because of this time. (Reporter asked) What are your future suggestions for remedying party affairs? (Answer) I have always advocated that only sincere unity can solve the problem of party affairs. However, I regret that my words are insignificant and not understood by many comrades. In 1927, I advocated cooperation between Ning, Han, and Shanghai to form a special committee, but it failed due to opposition from some comrades. In 1928, I telegraphed the central government from overseas, advocating cooperation between Hu, Wang, and Jiang, but it was also obstructed and could not be realized. The Extraordinary Conference was established this year, based on the principle of sincere unity and no factionalism, to achieve the goal of overthrowing dictatorship and unifying the party. It has already achieved considerable success. In the future, we should continue to proceed according to this principle. Now that the national crisis is getting deeper, we must unite as one to deal with foreign enemies. However, there are still some comrades who do not understand this principle and are obsessing over old accounts and using emotions. I am of meager talent and unable to persuade my comrades, and I am deeply ashamed. I only hope that Mr. Hu, Wang, and Jiang can put aside everything at this time and come to Beijing together. These three gentlemen all have special status in the party and are respected by party members from all sides. If they can meet and discuss, everything will be easily resolved. As for the past merits, demerits, rights, and wrongs, Mr. Jiang has already resigned to take responsibility, and I think it can be brought to an end. For the sake of the party and the country, at this time, we must work hard to develop a new situation. Everything in the past is like dying yesterday, and everything in the future is the beginning. The survival and honor of the party and the country are truly tied to this. I hope these three gentlemen can act quickly and resolutely to resolve the national crisis. If all three gentlemen can come together, I will do my best to follow them. Otherwise, if my strength is not enough to fulfill my wishes and I cannot save the situation, I will only temporarily not ask about party affairs.

Pan Gongzhan Resigns as

Director of the Municipal Party Committee and Social Affairs Bureau

Frequent Labor and Business Disputes

Overwhelmed with Handling

Pan Gongzhan, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Committee and Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, telegraphed the Central Committee yesterday requesting to resign from his position as a member of the Municipal Executive Committee and sent a letter to the Municipal Party Committee for review. At the same time, he submitted a request to Mayor Zhang to resign from his substantive position as Director of the Social Affairs Bureau to recuperate. His telegram is recorded below.

Telegram to the Central Committee To the Organization Department of the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters

transferred to the Central Executive Committee, Pan Gongzhan has been mistakenly in charge of the Shanghai municipal party affairs for nearly four years. Usually, due to holding both political affairs positions, he has put in less effort. Upon introspection, he feels deeply indebted. Since the Shenyang Incident, the pressure of foreign troubles has led to a surge of student movements. Guidance and persuasion have all failed. Even the party headquarters has been destroyed, and blame has been placed on him. Pan Gongzhan has followed the overall executive and supervisory committee members of the city in requesting a general resignation, but has not yet received instructions. In the past half-month, the party affairs disputes have been increasing day by day, and the abnormal organization cannot be investigated. He believes that while the Central Committee is celebrating unity, this city is showing division. If this continues, it will be like suicide. Moreover, in the business and labor sectors, the storms have suddenly risen, with one side fighting the other, and there is no peace. The breakdown of organizations and the mutual disputes between labor and management, at a time when the effectiveness of the law has lost its authority, are inevitably bound to happen. At this time of internal and external troubles, how can we bear to see this disintegration? He believes that he is weak and unable to turn the tide. He dares to pour out his innermost feelings and begs the conference to grant him permission to resign from his position as a member of the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee, so as to avoid further mistakes and relieve the burden. He cannot help but await orders in fear. Furthermore, from this day on, Pan Gongzhan will no longer be responsible for the Shanghai municipal party affairs. In the future, in his spare time, he will still contribute his humble suggestions as a party member for selection and will never dare to be lazy and idle. This is combined and clarified. Pan Gongzhan bows, You.

Letter to the Mayor Regarding resignation, Pan

Gongzhan has been mistakenly in charge of the bureau affairs for more than four years. Fortunately, with the instructions of Your Excellency and the support of society, the construction projects have been able to proceed in an orderly manner, and the statistical work has achieved a considerable position. Usually, he has followed the laws in mediating labor-management disputes and reorganizing various organizations to gradually stabilize social order and eliminate the gap between business and labor. Now, although all facilities are roughly in place, his weak body and mind are already exhausted. Unexpectedly, recently, storms have suddenly risen in the Shanghai business and labor sectors, and what has been gradually brought into order over the years will be destroyed without remainder. He believes that he is weak, and future governance will not be possible. Therefore, he dares to pour out his innermost feelings and begs Your Excellency to examine and approve his resignation from his substantive position and quickly select personnel to take over so as to recuperate and avoid further mistakes. He cannot help but await orders in gratitude. Respectfully presented to Mayor Zhang.

Workers at the Commercial Press

Clashed Again Yesterday

Both Sides Injured

The dispute among workers at the printing plant of the Commercial Press on Baoshan Road, the details of which were recorded in yesterday's newspaper, occurred again yesterday morning. Both sides were beaten and injured, and both were sent to the hospital for treatment. The details are recorded below.

Course of the Conflict After the dispute occurred

in the Commercial Press the afternoon before yesterday, workers Huang Rongqing, Hu Jinshan, Bao Yongde, Bao Achang, Li Yiqing, Jiang Guoli, Che Qu Xian, Xu Tongkang, and others were detained by the military police and temporarily held in the military police group joint office of the Huzhou Guild Hall on Huiwen Road, Zhabei. Yesterday morning, the publishing industry workers' union reorganization committee prepared an official letter and went to inquire. They learned that the detained workers had been taken by the Fifth District Public Security Bureau to the military police group office. At 8 AM, when the printing plant of the Commercial Press started work, representatives of the workers heard that Hou Dachun, Wang Changyuan, and others wanted to convene a meeting in the factory. The entire group rushed to the union and clashed with the security team. Union supervisors Hou Dachun, Wang Changyuan, and Yan Yongquan were severely beaten and injured. Workers Zhang Wenkui, Feng Chenggen, Xu Amao, Luo Dazhi, Ni Dalin, Han Daocheng, Huang Chang Er, and others were also injured. Hou Dachun and Wang Changyuan were sent to Baolong Hospital by car, and Yan Yongquan was sent to Jisheng Hospital by car. The remaining injured workers were treated at Tongren Hospital. Hou and Wang were injured in the head, and their conditions were serious. Yan's injuries were also very critical.

Arrested and Sent to Court When the conflict occurred between the two sides

yesterday morning, the Fifth District Public Security Bureau, led by Inspector Gao, dispatched police to suppress the situation and detained workers Wang Bin, Wu Youfu, Li Nanqin, Wu Chengshi, Sun Abing, Qiao Zhonghe, Qian Tingliang, Zhao Guisheng, and others at the district office. At about 1 PM, together with Huang Rongqing, Hu Jinshan, and others who were taken from the military police group joint office, they were sent to the local court. Those who were injured and treated in the hospital were summoned by the court.

What Was Heard After the Incident After the workers' dispute occurred

at the Commercial Press, various sectors paid close attention. It was heard that someone had mediated in order to avoid expanding the storm. The publishing industry workers' union reorganization committee also submitted reports to the municipal government, the garrison headquarters, and the municipal party headquarters, requesting punishment for the perpetrators and informing the workers to work with peace of mind.

According to the New Voice News Agency, the publishing industry workers' union issued a responsible report stating that a few members of the municipal party committee colluded with undesirable elements of the Commercial Press branch to hold an extraordinary meeting and illegally produced a workers' delegation. The union submitted a request to the Social Affairs Bureau and the municipal party committee to ban it. Later, according to the instructions of the Social Affairs Bureau, permission was granted for the ban. However, the municipal party committee shielded the workers' delegation and ignored the request. As for stopping activities and sending personnel to reorganize, all were members of the workers' delegation. Now, due to the joint proclamation of the municipal government and the garrison headquarters banning illegal organizations, the delegation should be illegal. Therefore, it will not be accepted. The report was submitted to the Central Government for thorough investigation and to await resolution quietly.

British-Owned Public Buses

Completely Stopped Yesterday

Workers Went from Slowdown to Actual Strike

Company Announcement Limits Registration to Today

Attack on Staff and Destruction of Vehicles Occurred Yesterday

After a slowdown by all ticket sellers of the British-owned public bus company, yesterday it turned into an actual strike, and buses on all routes completely stopped. The company issued an announcement limiting registration to today, or else the job will be terminated. There were also incidents of assaulting staff and destroying vehicles. The various situations are recorded below.

Maintaining Traffic In order to maintain traffic, the

company had ticket checkers and others act as agents in the morning to force operation. Route 1, Jing’an Temple to the shooting range, was shortened to Old Shooting Range Road, operating 14 buses. Route 9, Jing’an Temple to the power plant, was shortened to Tilanqiao, operating 10 buses. Later, because striking workers used force to stop it, the police, in order to prevent accidents, ordered the company to temporarily stop driving. As a result, the one-nine buses that had been operating in the morning all stopped operating.

Assaulting Staff At 10 AM yesterday morning, ticket seller number

141, Cheng Tingliang, was working on the 9th route bus, driving to the intersection of Hart Road and Avenue Foch, when he was discovered by striking ticket sellers. They regarded him as disrupting strike discipline and dragged Cheng to the middle of the road, throwing lime bags at him, resulting in his injury. He was sent to the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road by the police. It was heard that he had lost his sight. At 12:15 PM, the number 80 bus driver was suspected by striking workers of secretly guaranteeing the ticket checkers in the company and was beaten by the crowd in the company. Mr. Dan, a Western staff member of the company, tried to persuade them, but he was slightly injured. The glass of a route 1 bus was also smashed while driving on Jing’an Temple Road.

Workers' Meeting After all striking ticket sellers

petitioned Yao Zengmo, the Chinese chief inspector of the Shanghai Municipal Council, the day before yesterday, they held a discussion meeting in front of the company on Connaught Road yesterday morning. It was heard that the result of the discussion was: (1) If ticket seller number 1 is not released, all will be willing to be the backing and insist on continuing the slowdown; (2) Those who disrupt discipline will be dealt with severely.

Complete Shutdown After 10 AM yesterday, route

1 Jing’an Temple to the power plant, route 2 Eryangjing Bridge to the shooting range, route 4 Xujiahui to the airport, route 5 Sanmaoge Bridge to the North Railway Station, route 6 the shooting range to Route 6, route 7 Caojiadu to Jiaotong University, route 9 Jing’an Temple to the power plant, route 10 Caojiadu to Yinxiang Port completely stopped operating. Passengers felt quite inconvenienced. As a result, trams were very crowded, and rickshaws were three times as profitable.

Company Announcement The British-owned public bus company

announced yesterday: For the matter of the announcement, ticket seller number 1 of this company has been arrested for inciting a strike and will be punished by the police in accordance with the laws of the Republic of China. Starting tomorrow (December 27, 1931), all employees who do not report to work at this company will have their positions terminated by this company, and they must return their uniforms and other items to receive their wages.

Attitudes of Labor and Management Ticket sellers told the New Voice News Agency reporter yesterday that

all 280 of us were newly recruited by the company, and our monthly salary is 23 yuan. Usually, the company oppresses workers quite a lot. If we do not jump the red card or open the door before arriving at the station, we will be recorded, and after three major mistakes, we will be dismissed. This time, it was purely to help ticket seller number 1. If he is not released for one day, then we will not return to work for one day. According to company news, they plan to follow the previous method of the old ticket sellers' strike. If they do not return to work today, they will all be dismissed and new workers will be hired to continue working.

The Illness of Central Committee Member Cai Yuanpei

Was Hospitalized Yesterday to Treat Arm Injury

Central Committee member Cai Yuanpei was injured in the student petition conflict at the Central Party Headquarters. After being treated at the Central Hospital in Nanjing for a few days, he moved to Shanghai and was treated at his residence. Initially, his injuries were only swelling and redness in his arm and bruises on his back, which did not seem very serious. With slight recuperation and treatment, he should have recovered soon. Unexpectedly, after arriving in Shanghai, the pain in his arm worsened, and it was difficult to extend and flex it. The bruises on his back had not subsided either. After a medical examination by Dr. Bei, it was said that there might be a fracture in the bones of his right arm. If it is not treated quickly, there will be future problems. Therefore, he was moved to a certain hospital yesterday to use X-rays to examine the inside of his arm injury and give fundamental treatment. According to Cai's family member who is caring for him, Cai is in good spirits while ill. However, he is old, and he still feels dizzy from being hit on the head. The bruises on his arms and back make it difficult for him to move. Doctors have forbidden him from reading books, so his newspapers are read aloud to him by his caregivers. Although he is very concerned about the recent situation and the national crisis, he does not seem to want to be too involved in actual politics.

Niu Yongjian Resigns and Comes to Shanghai

Niu Tiesheng, Minister of the Bureau of Evaluation of the Examination Yuan, resigned from his substantive position because he was better at military affairs and did not want to engage in the literary battle. The Eastern Province was lost, and difficulties were imminent. Niu was extremely angry and submitted his resignation to fight against Japan. However, the national government instructed him to stay, which was not approved. It is now known that Niu submitted a second resignation and left Beijing for Shanghai yesterday. He will return to his residence at No. 90 Zhifeng Lane, Huanlong Road, to rest temporarily and will plan with people in Shanghai to coordinate the rescue of the national crisis.

Yan and Feng Telegraph Wang, Coming to Beijing at the Same Time

According to the Guowen News Agency, members of the Central Committee from the Northwest, Yan Xishan, Feng Yuxiang, Zhao Daiwen, Liu Shouzhong, and others telegraphed Mr. Wang Jingwei, a member of the Guangdong Committee staying in Shanghai, yesterday, expressing concern for his illness and saying that, in the face of the national crisis, they hope that he will work hard to attend the meeting and jointly decide national affairs. We are waiting for Mr. to arrive in Beijing, and we will set off to come south at the same time. It is heard that Wang also telegraphed Feng and Yan yesterday.

Pudong Rihua Textile Mill

Complete Stoppage of Work in the Weaving Room

Japanese Capitalists' Various Oppressions

Increasing Workload, Reducing Wages

Unwarranted Detention of Two Workers

Yesterday's Appeal to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs

Reason for the Stoppage: According to Guomin News Agency, the Rihua Textile Mill in Pudong is run by Japanese capitalists. Since the Northeast Incident occurred, and the entire country severed economic ties with Japan, Japanese yarn has been greatly affected. The mill's management has been provoking workers in every way, dismissing hundreds of workers without cause. On the 24th of this month, the management implemented another malicious plan, increasing the workload for all female workers in the weaving room. Those who previously managed three looms are now required to manage four. The wage for each piece of cloth woven, previously 56 cents, has now been reduced to 50 cents. The mill also ordered female collaborators Zhang Fuying and Hu Azhen to force the workers to work. Subsequently, they falsely reported to the police station, leading to the detention of workers Lu Xiaomei and Ni Jinxiu. All the workers, having endured enough, unanimously stopped working and gathered at the union to hold a meeting, demanding: (1) the release of the detained female workers; (2) the reinstatement of the dismissed female workers; (3) the restoration of the original working conditions. The union immediately reported the situation urgently to higher authorities and sent representatives to negotiate. The factory management's attitude was firm, and no progress was made. The unrest is likely to escalate.

Submitted to the Bureau of Social Affairs: Regarding the Urgent Report, Since the violent Japanese seized our Eastern Provinces, the cruel capitalists have also taken advantage of the situation, dismissing hundreds of workers without cause. Our association, considering international relations and fearing falling into their trap, has repeatedly endured the pain and reported the situation to your bureau for record. Unexpectedly, on the 24th of this month, the management implemented another malicious plan, intending to dismiss over a hundred more workers in the weaving room, and further increasing the workload while reducing wages. For example, those who usually managed one or two machines will now have to manage three to four. The wage for each piece of cloth, previously 56 cents, will now only be 50 cents. They ordered the female collaborators and foremen Hu Azhen and Zhang Fuying to announce this to the workers and enforce it. The workers, noting that since the opening of the factory, each person has managed at most two machines, and it is physically impossible to manage three or four, and that increasing the workload while reducing wages is unreasonable, believe that the management is intentionally destroying them and oppressing them without cause, which is unacceptable. Therefore, they asked Hu Azhen and others to convey to the management a plea for them to reconsider and withdraw the order. Unexpectedly, Hu Azhen and others not only refused to accept the workers' opinions but also relied on the management's power to insult and scold them, leading to conflicts in language with the workers. They then falsely reported to the Third District Police Station that they had been beaten, resulting in the arrest of workers Lu Xiaomei and Ni Jinxiu, who were sent to the court and have not yet been released. Currently, all 400+ workers in the weaving room, seeing this situation, are filled with righteous indignation. If no appropriate solution is found, they will be forced to resign together. Our association believes this matter is of great importance, so we submit this report to your bureau, requesting that you promptly send representatives to mediate with the management, and also appeal to the local court to immediately release Lu Xiaomei and Ni Jinxiu to avoid injustice and appease public anger. We await your urgent instructions. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs.

Collective Petition: The New Voice Society reports that all 400+ female workers in the weaving room went to the local court at 10 a.m. the day before yesterday to petition for the immediate release of the arrested female workers. They were received by the clerk, who advised them to disperse and wait for processing. However, the female workers were unwilling to leave and insisted on the release. The female workers Bao Cuidi and Cai Fuzhen were questioned and released, but Chen Xiaomei and Ni Jinxiu were not released because their case involved causing injury through assault. All the female workers were forced to return to the factory temporarily to arrange bail.

Dismissal of Workers: The Rihua Textile Mill announced yesterday morning that it is currently affected by the current situation and the market is declining. To avoid causing suffering to the workers, the mill has tried its best to maintain operations, as the workers know. However, the situation cannot be resolved quickly, and the factory faces extraordinary difficulties. In this transitional period, it is necessary to find ways to improve. Unexpectedly, workers engaged in fighting. Therefore, the following workers who caused the trouble are dismissed: Chen Baoying, Tang Jinda, Lu Xiaomei, Han Xiuzhen, Pan Xiuying, Fu Wenzhen, Ni Jinxiu, Bao Cuidi, Shao A'gen, Cai Xiaomei, and Cai Fuzhen. They must leave the workshop within ten days.

Authorities' Advice: Zhang, the District Chief of the Third District Police Station of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and armed police officers from the Fourth Company of the Police Brigade went to maintain order. District Chief Zhang, along with staff from the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, personally went to advise the female workers: (1) Regarding the arrested female workers, wait for the court to handle it according to law; (2) Regarding the reduction of wages and the increase in the number of machines, wait for the Party and government organs to mediate according to law; (3) Hope that the workers will resume work first. However, the workers insisted on refusing. The union scheduled a general meeting last night to discuss solutions.

Overseas Chinese in Yunfu

Organize a National Salvation Association Aboard Ship

Donate Funds to Support Soldiers

Issue a Declaration

On December 1st, there were over 200 overseas Chinese passengers on the Blue Funnel Line's Chindara, which departed from Hobart. Daily radio messages from the ship reported that the Japanese invaders were plundering our country and slaughtering our compatriots with increasing ferocity. Upon hearing the news, the overseas Chinese were filled with righteous indignation and wanted to annihilate the Japanese before eating. They proposed organizing a National Salvation Association to resist Japan and unify their will. Temporary officers were elected, including: Chairman Huang Lanrui, Secretaries Shi Qifeng, Huang Shizhou, Yu Linghe, Wen Jiliang Hong, Treasurers Tan Yangzhao, Huang Gonglou, Propagandists Huang Bobo, Wu Shihe, Yu Jinghe, Yang Zhang, Cai Hong, Situ Da, Yu Qichang, Disciplinarians Huang Gongce, Zheng Zanxian, Luo Niande, Li Lin, Liu Yong, Huang Hua, General Affairs Wu Yuechuan, Li Yu, and Receptionists Yu Zhaozhong, Chen Rongcong, Tang Yizuo. They immediately divided into departments to handle affairs and drafted a declaration to resist Japan. They chose 8 p.m. on the 15th to hold the inaugural meeting. At that time, except for a few who did not know what the country was, everyone enthusiastically attended. The meeting order was: (1) Shi Qifeng, as the master of ceremonies, led the audience to stand and bow three times to the national flag; (2) The entire audience observed three minutes of silence to mourn the compatriots who died in the Northeast; (3) The chairman was invited to take his seat and announce the reasons for the meeting; (4) Speeches were given by the ship's doctor, Zeng Ziming, the ship's compradore, Liang Hong, as well as Situ Da, Huang Bobo, Wu Shihe, Yang Zhang, Huang Shizhou, Yu Linghe, Luo Niande, Zheng Zanxian, Yu Qichang, Huang Gongce, and Shi Qifeng. Dr. Zeng explained the reasons for the loss of the Northeast and the Japanese plans for our country in the future, and encouraged compatriots to make a great determination to resist Japan to the end. Liang Hong announced the intense anti-Japanese movements in Guangdong, Hong Kong, Shanghai, and the losses suffered by industry and commerce since China's unified economic severance with Japan. Huang Bobo strongly criticized the lack of responsibility of the Chinese people, their shirking of responsibility when things happen, and their fondness for making meaningless criticisms as the biggest weaknesses. If we want to save the country, we must correct our past mistakes, understand our responsibilities, and earnestly shoulder them. He also played a military-style harmonica, which was慷慨激昂. The patriotic atmosphere throughout the meeting was extremely tense. The others all gave encouraging speeches. After each speech, applause thundered. (5) Anti-Japanese regulations were approved: (A) No one should land at any Japanese port; (B) No one should buy Japanese goods; (C) Telegraph to reject Japan; (6) Slogans were shouted: (1) Down with Japanese imperialism; (2) Abolish unequal treaties; (3) Economic severance with Japan; (4) Promote peaceful unification; (5) Long live the success of resisting Japan and saving the country; (6) Long live the Republic of China; (7) Yu Qichang thanked the guests; (8) The meeting adjourned. On the 19th, the ship arrived in Yokohama, and on the 21st, it arrived in Kobe. The disciplinarians strictly monitored, and no passenger landed or traded with the Japanese. The Kobe Chinese Association sent several copies of the Shen Bao newspaper. It was learned that General Ma Zhanshan's brave soldiers were fiercely fighting the Japanese in the frozen lands. Many domestic groups were vying to raise funds to support them. Everyone believed that it was the undeniable responsibility of all citizens. Therefore, they launched another fundraising campaign to慰勞 the soldiers at the front. First, the ship's compradore, Liang Hong, generously donated 56 yuan. Then, the passengers were asked to donate freely. A total of 145 yuan and 32 yuan and 6.5 cents were raised. The funds were directly remitted to General Ma Zhanshan through the Shanghai Bank of Communications, and the names of the donors were published in the Shanghai Shen Bao newspaper for one day to show good faith. According to investigations, the commercial and industrial conditions of various Japanese ports along the coast have plummeted due to the boycott by our country. In Yokohama, 80% of the Chinese residents have returned to China. The Chinese district is now deserted. After 8 p.m., there are no pedestrians on the streets. In Kobe, all Chinese-run businesses have completely shut down. After waiting a few days to complete the liquidation, they will pack their bags and return home. This is truly an unprecedented phenomenon. The hearts of the people have not died; can the Japanese bandits not be destroyed? Declaration of the National Salvation Association of Overseas Chinese Returning from Blue Funnel Line's Chindara: China is the China of the Chinese people. Any nation in the world, regardless of size or strength, must be able to maintain the sacred sovereignty and territory of its country in order to be called a country. Otherwise, it is merely a colony; in short, it is a slave. Our Chinese nation has a history of over 4,000 years and is a pioneer in world civilization. Due to its inherent simple customs and benevolence towards people and things, it has often been taken advantage of by foreign tribes. The Manchus invaded the Central Plains and implemented a poisonous policy of愚民, and our people groaned under the despotic iron hoof for over 200 years, almost becoming weak and helpless. Fortunately, heaven helped China, and the revolution succeeded. We could have worked hard to govern well, but unfortunately, the hearts of the people were not awakened, leading to strongmen stealing the country and foreign invasions coming one after another. Like a bolt from the blue, the Japanese invaded and occupied our Northeast, killing our compatriots and creating an unprecedentedly tragic history for mankind, committing a great injustice to world peace. Compatriots, the Japanese have already shown their hideous faces and are coming to devour us. Can the people of all of China endure this? Our ancestors preserved the integrity of the land and independent sovereignty with iron and blood and handed it over to us. Are we going to be submissive, allowing ourselves to be slaughtered, and hand over a dog-like slave's humble servitude to our descendants? Are we not human? Compatriots, please rise up quickly, stand together under the banner of resisting Japan and saving the country, and vow to use the united strength of the entire nation to preserve the integrity of the land and the independent sovereignty that our ancestors handed over to us. As the saying goes, "Better to be a shattered piece of jade than a whole tile." Only by being able to die on the battlefield and flatten the Japanese islands can we be considered iron-blooded men. Even if we are pierced by bullets and dismembered by knives and spears, we are defending the country, and only then can we be considered worthy descendants of our ancestors. Today, as we arrive in Japan, it is like enemies meeting, and our eyes are especially clear. We regret that the time has not yet come to kill them all and avenge our compatriots who died in the Northeast. However, at the very least, we must vigorously implement economic severance. Therefore, we have organized a National Salvation Association, firstly to express the great determination of the passengers and crew on this ship to resist Japan, and secondly to support the anti-Japanese associations at home and abroad. All our compatriots should share the enemy's hatred and observe the anti-Japanese regulations approved by this association. If there are any who betray their own kind, recognize thieves as their fathers, and dare to trade with the Japanese, this association will treat them with appropriate civilized means. Everyone should cherish themselves. This declaration is hereby made. December 14th, 20th year of the Republic of China.

Minzhi Association

Telegraphs Li, Requesting Insistence on the Original Proposal

The Minzhi Association telegraphed Li Xiehe, stating: To Honorable Mr. Xiehe and all the gentlemen, we deeply admire your proposal on the four items at the First Plenary Session of the First Central Executive Committee, which concern the fundamental rights of the people and express your loyalty. It has been heard that the meeting passed the first item, and the rest are being discussed together. Upon investigation, only the first item in the proposal is an empty principle, and the most important item is the second item in the proposed case, allowing the people to freely organize groups or political parties. The freedom to form parties is the most important element of democratic politics. Otherwise, if only one party is allowed to exist in a country, acting alone, it will block its ears and obscure its vision and cannot benefit from the effectiveness of others' experiences. The people will also have no way to express their different opinions, and democratic politics will be difficult to achieve. This is the first reason. At a time of chaos, we sincerely hope that the entire nation, from top to bottom, will work together to build up its strength. To achieve this goal, the only way is to allow the people to freely organize political groups, from small combinations to form large combinations, in order to gather the flow of all people and jointly face the national crisis. This is the second reason. The absence of parties outside the Party has already been broken in fact. The Communist Party and the Third Party exist prominently and are not easily shaken. They either occupy remote areas and establish governments, or they manipulate unions and display resistance. Since it is impossible to eliminate these groups, they are trying to destroy those who use peaceful means for rational organization, forcing them to lose their foothold. This is no less than driving away fish and birds for the sake of the abyss. Thinking of the future, we are shivering. This is the third reason. Your proposition is appropriate and just for both the country and the Party. We earnestly hope that you will continue your efforts and persist in your original proposal. All patriotic people are willing to be your support. Furthermore, the organization of this association takes the business and academic communities as its backbone and advocates using peaceful methods to achieve the goal of exciting democracy. The details of the establishment are fully reported in the Shanghai newspaper. We humbly report and hope for your understanding. The Shanghai People's Rule Association.

Order in Wuyuan is About to be Restored

Shanghai Wuyuan Compatriot Association Received a Reply Telegram from the Anhui Provincial Government Yesterday

The Wuyuan Compatriot Association in Shanghai received a reply telegram from the Anhui Provincial Government yesterday, stating: Investigation of the situation of bandits disturbing Wucheng. Previously, according to repeated telegram reports from Division Commander Ruan, we immediately telegraphed to order Brigade Commander Zhang of that division to quickly lead his troops to suppress the bandits. Now, according to the telegram report from Division Commander Hao, the bandits attacked Wucheng, and the police force resisted ineffectively and withdrew from the east gate, resulting in looting. The office has already telegraphed to order Brigade Commander Zhang to lead Wu and Wang's two regiments to return from Raoerdun and pursue north. At the same time, the engineer battalion is on alert in Jingdezhen, and the battalion commander is dispatched to lead two companies of soldiers to Wucheng to restore order. It is also reported in the telegram from Brigade Commander Zhang that, according to the confessions of the farmer bandits, the bandit forces number about 2,000, with 700-800 guns. During the attack on Wucheng, they used ladders to climb the city walls. After capturing the city, they looted and fled back to Haikou. It has been confirmed that Qiaozao has fled south. Order in Wucheng should be restored soon. It is also planned to thoroughly clear out the accumulated bandits in the area east of De and south of Wu in order to alleviate the concerns of southern Anhui. Besides ordering them to actively search and suppress the bandits as soon as possible, we are replying to you. Chen Diaoyuan.

More Local News on the Following Page

Local News Two

The Hull of the Dade Ship is Towed to Shanghai

The Entire Ship is Damaged Beyond Use

Towed into the Ruirong Shipyard

Ship's Hull Enters Dock: The hull of the Dade, a merchant ship of the Dada Company, which was burned in a fire at Qiwang, was left in the Hupu area to deal with the task of recovering the bodies of the deceased passengers and crew members, as the company was salvaging. Now that many bodies have been recovered and successively photographed and collected, the hull of the burnt Dade ship has entered water on the shallow beach of Qiwang. Therefore, the Shanghai Maritime Bureau sent the Daqing ship owner to take the Dahe ship to tow it. The hull of the Dade ship has been brought to Shanghai. Yesterday, the hull of the ship was towed into the Ruirong factory for temporary mooring in order to enter the dock to dismantle the machinery.

No Goods Remain: The goods in each cabin of the Dade ship were almost completely burned after the fire. Even the remaining goods at the bottom of the cabin were looted by fishing boats and pirate ships in the area. Therefore, when the hull of the Dade ship was towed back to Shanghai this time, the Shanghai Maritime Bureau sent personnel to inspect the ship and found that there were no remaining goods left at the bottom of each cabin. Even the belongings and luggage left by the passengers and crew members in the cabins had been burned a long time ago. When it was towed back, it was only an empty hull.

Machinery Damaged: The extent of damage of this fire on the Dade ship is even greater than the previous fire on the Daji ship. Although the engines and machinery inside the ship were not burned, they have been damaged by the fire. The engine parts have no power to start. Technicians from the Maritime Bureau and the Ruirong factory have determined that the machinery in the Dade ship can no longer be used.

Discussing the Aftermath: The Maritime Bureau has decided to convene a board meeting to determine the disposal method for the aftermath of the Dade ship case. Currently, there are only one or two directors in Shanghai, and the rest are not in Shanghai. The Bureau has already issued a notice convening a board meeting. When the directors from various places arrive in Shanghai, they will discuss: (1) the issue of disposing of the Dade ship's hull; (2) the issue of adding new ships to supplement the routes; (3) the issue of providing compensation to the deceased crew members and passengers. At the same time, they have submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications to send personnel to Shanghai to inspect the existing scheduled ships to ensure caution.

Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities

Recent News on the Preparation of the Pudong Water Plant

Re-Creating the Budget and Submitting it to the Government for Approval

To the Honorable Shanghai Municipal Government: The need for tap water in various districts of Pudong for public drinking and fire protection is very urgent. It has been decided to establish a water plant. The Bureau of Public Utilities was ordered to prepare it and immediately drafted a plan and surveyed and determined that the public land at Laiyidu Youlong Road Taoyuanzhai would be the site for the construction of the plant. Recently, it also met with the Land Bureau to purchase the land owned by the Li and Gu families nearby to meet the current layout and the needs of future expansion. Recently, the Bureau also plans to build a water tower on the public land at No. 5 Laiyidu Street (i.e., the current location of the city-run artesian well). An observation deck will be built on the top of the tower, and a business office will be built on the base of the tower, estimated to cost over 30,000 yuan. According to the rapid filtration pool plan originally approved by the Bureau, the water tower was not included in order to save expenses. However, after detailed consideration, it was felt that a small-scale water plant would not be able to average the pressure without a water tower, which would inevitably consume more mechanical power. It is not advisable. Furthermore, the Hutungbang artesian well can also use the tower to store water first for fire protection purposes. Therefore, it was re-submitted to the Municipal Government for approval to add this equipment. However, the total cost of the water plant was originally estimated to be over 160,000 yuan. Now, due to the purchase of land and the addition of a water tower, as well as the increase in the price of machinery and pipes, it will have to increase to 280,000 yuan. It is understood that the Bureau has re-created the budget and submitted it to the Municipal Government. It will be able to start construction next year.

Owners Self-Install Water Supply Equipment

Go to the Public Security Bureau to Renew Licenses Quickly

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has registered nearly 500 self-installed water supply equipment by owners in the city. It has been stipulated that the price licenses must be exchanged for new licenses uniformly during the period from December 1 to December 31 each year. Those who have received a license for less than six months will be exchanged for free. Those who have received it for more than six months but less than one year will pay half the fee (50 cents). It is understood that 3/4 of the owners have completed the procedures for renewing their licenses this year. The remaining 1/4 must bring their old licenses and go to the Bureau to exchange for new licenses before the end of this month, December 31. Otherwise, a 20% late fee (50 cents) will be added for each day of delay.
