Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Overview of the Commercial Library in its 20th Year

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Commercial Library has been established for nearly ten years. It has always been open to the public, so people from all walks of life come to the library to read or borrow books for reference. It is greatly welcomed. Now, feeling that shop employees do not have time to come to the library during the day to borrow books, a delivery department has been added since November, delivering books by bicycle every day. Therefore, the library's work is becoming increasingly busy. It is divided into five departments: general affairs, cataloging, cashier, reference, and delivery. According to this year's statistics, 2,246 Chinese books and 318 Western books were added. There are currently 337 kinds of Chinese magazines, with approximately 4,044 copies received throughout the year, 90% of which were donated by various bookstores and institutions. There are a total of 98 kinds of Western magazines, with 1,176 copies received throughout the year, 70% of which were also donated. This year, excluding the relocation of the library, year-end closing, and holidays, the library was open for 277 days throughout the year, with a total of 57,319 visitors, an average of 207 people per day. Due to a lack of statistics, it is estimated that 25,901 copies of daily newspapers were read in the library. 13,760 copies were borrowed from outside the library, an average of approximately 140 copies borrowed per day. The delivery department has 173 borrowers, delivering to an average of 30 locations per day.

Pig Boats Must First Stop at Wusong for Inspection

Permits will be issued starting January 1st of next year.

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau announced that, in order to protect the health of citizens and eliminate plague-infected meat, the Bureau has established a "Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Pig Boat Inspection and Release Permit." Starting on January 1, 1932, all pig boats passing through Wusong must dock along the riverbank for inspection by the inspectors from the Bureau's Wusong Rendering Plant. If any diseased or dead pigs are found, the dead pigs shall be detained for rendering to prevent clandestine slaughter and sale, and compensation will be given in accordance with regulations to show consideration. If no dead pigs are found, or if dead pigs have already been detained, the aforementioned inspection and release permit will be issued immediately to facilitate commercial transport. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government for record, the Public Security Bureau has been instructed to order the water patrol team to assist at any time. This announcement is hereby made for general information. (December 26, 1931)

After the Collapse of Yongda Bank

Shareholders Sue Manager

Accusation of Fraud and Embezzlement

Shareholders Ye Zhensheng and Wu Qizhou of the closed Yongda Bank recently hired lawyer Chao Kun to file a lawsuit with the First Special District Court, accusing the bank's manager, He Zanxun from Zhejiang, and his cousin, He Yixun (a lawyer and accountant), of breach of trust, fraud, forging documents, and embezzling over 70,000 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Feng Shide presided over the preliminary hearing in the Criminal Division Two. He Zanxun was absent. His lawyer appeared in court and stated that he was unable to appear due to illness and requested a postponement. He Yixun also appeared with lawyer E Sen. The plaintiff, Ye Zhensheng, testified that Yongda Bank had a total of six shareholders, with a total capital of 88,000 taels of silver. The defendant, He Zanxun, was the manager. The bank was gradually emptied of over 83,000 taels of silver by He, leading to the bank's sudden collapse on November 7th. However, I was completely unaware of the collapse at the time, as I usually did not go to the bank. All matters were handled by the manager. It was not until the next day, the 8th, that I learned of Yongda's collapse. I immediately tried to find He Zanxun, but he refused to see me. I also learned that all of the bank's account books had been taken away by He Yixun. They were not handed over to accountant Chao Jimei until the 9th, so all of the account books had been falsified. Later, the Yongda Bank accounting staff reported to me that the later entries in the account books were all added at He Zanxun's direction. The second defendant, He Yixun, has no connection with Yongda Bank. How could he directly go to the bank to open the silver safe and take away the account books for falsification? Therefore, I am filing this lawsuit. All the details of Yongda Bank's collapse can only be clarified when He Zanxun appears in court. The defendant, He Yixun, testified that he worked as a lawyer and accountant. On the evening of November 7th, he received a phone call from his cousin, He Zanxun, asking him to go to Yongda Bank to discuss remedies. He went there, and Zanxun told him that the bank was unable to maintain itself because the shareholder Ye Zhensheng had used too much money, and it would inevitably collapse. He asked me to find a way to remedy the situation, but I had no way. It immediately collapsed, and entrusted lawyer Xie Fangling and accountant Chao Jimei to liquidate. The next day, the 8th, Xie and Chao personally went to Yongda Bank and took away the account books. I did not take them away. Accountant Chao Jimei can be summoned to testify about this matter. Judge Feng verified the testimony and ordered the case to be adjourned until the afternoon of January 5th next year for further hearing.

Riye Bank

Board of Directors Issue Investigated Again Yesterday

In the case of the collapse of Shanghai Riye Bank Gongfa Company, creditors requested confirmation that Ye Shantao and others were shareholders and held director responsibilities. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhao Zhenhai of the Third High Court opened a hearing again. The official asked lawyer Yan Luqing, the representative of the creditors, whether there were any objections to the statement submitted by the lawyers representing Chen Xingwu, Zhou Songqing, Zhao Qinbo, etc., denying that they were shareholders or directors. Lawyer Yan Luqing replied that his firm had not received a copy and could not respond. Moreover, an investigation revealed that Zhao Qinbo and others were indeed shareholders and directors. How could they deny it? The official then asked whether a formal judgment from the former French Concession court had been served. Yan replied that the judgment of the former French Concession court was written casually, which his firm considered very strange. Subsequently, lawyer Dong Yu stated that his firm also represented creditors who did not accept the ruling of the former French Concession court, requesting confirmation that Ye Shantao and others were shareholders and directors of Gongfa Company, and requesting that the shareholders be ordered to bear the responsibility for prompt repayment. He also unanimously agreed with the former French Concession court's judgment on Huang's living expenses and lawyer Tan Yigong's fees. Lawyers Dong Chi and Bian Jialu, (represented by Huang Cengfu), Wang Shizong, etc., also made the same request. Then, lawyer Yang Zhihao, representing Zhao Qinbo, a director and shareholder of Gongfa Company, stated that Zhao Qinbo had already passed away. His heirs have now appointed my firm to file an appeal against the judgment of the former French Concession court on July 15th, which held Zhao Qinbo liable as a shareholder. An investigation reveals that he was merely a friend of Huang Chujiu and helped out, so he was given a monthly allowance for transportation expenses, but he was not a director. The official asked Zhao Qinbo that, since he was not a shareholder, why was his name on the shareholder list? Lawyer Yang replied that he feared he was fabricated by Huang Chujiu, etc. Lawyer Wu Zhiping, representing Chen Xingwu, Zhou Songqing, etc., disagreed with the former French Concession court's judgment that Chen and Zhou were liable as shareholders. Chen and Zhou were neither shareholders nor directors, and the transportation allowance was merely compensation for their efforts. Lawyer Lu Shaozong, representing Ye Shantao, also denied being a director or shareholder, with roughly the same intent. Lawyer Tan Yigong stated that his firm was entrusted by Huang's family because Huang's property was entirely handed over to the liquidation office, so his firm requested payment of fees from the former French Concession court, which was not unreasonable. Unexpectedly, he was also listed as an appellant by the creditors, which was very perplexing. Lawyer Liu Zuwang, representing Yuan Ludeng, a director and shareholder of Gongfa Company, argued that, although his client was a shareholder and director, the liquidator appointed by the former French Concession court had investigated and confirmed that his client was indeed unable to be responsible for repayment and had issued a ruling exempting him from execution. Since there was already such a ruling, the appeal should be dismissed. By this time, it was dusk. Judge Zhao announced that he would consider the matter further before adjourning the court.

Hankou

Morning Post Representative Goes to Beijing to Petition

Guarantee Freedom of Speech and Publication

Since its publication in 1926, the Hankou Morning Post participated in the National Revolution and was banned by the Northern Warlords. It was able to continue publication after the revolutionary army settled in Wuhan. This year, bandits are rampant and floods are frequent in Hubei Province. The newspaper's commentary slightly criticized the responsible authorities and was banned for the second time by the Hubei Provincial Government. Now, the newspaper's colleagues have come to Shanghai to issue a declaration and prepare for resumption of publication. Yesterday, they also sent representatives Chen Qifo, Bo Lian, and Wang Dingjiao to Beijing to petition the Fourth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee, requesting that freedom of speech and publication be absolutely guaranteed in the future.

Confucius Temple Park

Library to Open on Schedule

Public Education Center to be Built Soon

The Confucius Temple Park, located near the Penglai Market on Confucius Temple Road in the Nanshi district, which includes the Public Education Center and Library, was ordered by the Shanghai Municipal Government in February of this year to be jointly designed and renovated by the Municipal Works Bureau and the Education Bureau, transforming it into an educational park. Recently, most of the construction work in the park has been completed. At the site of the former Minglun Elementary School in the east corner, the Public Education Center is being rebuilt and preparations are being made to begin renovation of the library. The library is scheduled to open on January 10th, and the official opening of the park is expected to be realized by the end of February next year. The construction funds will be allocated from the education funds designated by the Municipal Government. It is reported that the cost of building the library, including construction, is 24,000 yuan, and the total cost of all renovations will be approximately 10,000 yuan. The estimated cost of renovating the Minglun Elementary School under construction is 8,000 yuan. The newly built library is scheduled to open on January 10th, allowing citizens to visit. The Education Bureau recently purchased over 12,000 volumes of ancient and modern books from various bookstores, which are currently being classified and cataloged and will be completed before the opening. The Education Bureau has issued an order to officially open the Confucius Temple by the end of February. The organization of the Public Education Center is divided into the General Affairs Group, which manages accounting, documents, and general affairs; the Lecture Group, which holds various academic and popular lectures; the Editing Group, which edits various popular reading materials and popular illustrations; the Exhibition Group, which exhibits various historical, geographical, natural history, and art models; and the Health Group, which guides the public to pay attention to hygiene and participate in sports activities.

House Tax and Road Repair Fee Issues

Taxpayers' Association Sends Letter to the Public Works Department

The Shanghai Concession Taxpayers' Chinese Association sent the following two letters to the Director-General of the Public Works Department of the Public Concession yesterday: (1) Sir, we have received a letter from Chunlai, No. 120 on Fuzhou Road, stating that at 10:00 AM on the 21st of this month, a Westerner from the Public Works Department came to our store to investigate the house ticket, claiming that the house tax could not be levied based on the monthly rent stated on the house ticket and that the house tax must be levied based on an estimated value. It has always been the standard to use the actual rent as the standard. How can it be increased arbitrarily and without limit, which is close to excessive taxation? We are sending this letter to request that the Public Works Department levy the house tax on our store at the original amount. We anxiously await your instructions, etc. The collection of municipal general taxes should be based on the actual rent. Now your bureau arbitrarily increases the rent to collect taxes, which is not proper. In view of the above, we are sending this letter to request that you investigate and correct it immediately. (2) Sir, we have received a letter from Dundacheng, Zhili Road, stating that we have received your letter and know that a section of Zhili Road on Wuxi Road is in disrepair. The Public Works Department has been notified, but the Public Works Department sent workers to repair only a one or two square foot area, and the rest has not yet been started. There are many vehicles entering and exiting this road, and there are often traffic jams. Our company's coal trucks also rely on this road. Because this road is not finished, we are afraid that it will cause trouble. We are sending this letter again to request that you immediately instruct the Public Works Department to speed up the construction, which we deeply hope for, etc. Since this road is an important road for vehicles entering and exiting, in order to avoid accidents, your bureau should immediately order repairs. In view of the above, we are sending this letter to request that you investigate and handle it, and live up to the trust of the taxpayers.

Biaohai Patrol Ship to Undergo Sea Trials Tomorrow

Chairman of the League of Nations Health Committee

Lachman Scheduled to Return to Geneva

Chairman Haas of the Communications Committee Arrives in Shanghai

Havas News Agency reported on the 26th that Dr. Lachman, Chairman of the League of Nations Health Committee, will leave Shanghai on Tuesday, travelling to Geneva via Siberia. Dr. Lachman arrived in China in mid-September and undertook numerous tasks, including making recommendations to the Economic Committee regarding the use of the League of Nations' various technical health agencies and the assistance that the Chinese government can obtain in formulating and implementing construction plans, and coordinating epidemic prevention affairs in flood-stricken areas. The first level was a request from the National Government to the Council of the League of Nations, and the second level was a request from the Ministry of Health to the Council. Regarding epidemic prevention, the National Government Flood Relief Committee received letters from the governments of French Vietnam, Poland, Spain, the Dutch East Indies, India, Denmark, and others, offering assistance. Dr. Lachman, on behalf of the Council of the League of Nations, coordinated these efforts. To date, League of Nations Health Committee members Professor Sicca and Dr. Huang are still working in the disaster area for the Epidemic Prevention Committee. In addition, Professor Stampar, a well-known expert on health issues, will come to China in mid-January of next year to take on this work. The League of Nations Health Committee's recommendations to the Chinese government are based on the results of two on-site investigations. These investigations were very thorough. The part concerning medical education was undertaken by Professor Flexner from Denmark, and the part concerning the establishment of national import epidemic prevention offices was undertaken by Professor Long, Director of the League of Nations' Singapore Epidemic Prevention Office. In addition, Dr. Brook from the League of Nations Health Committee has been serving in the Nanjing Ministry of Health since July of last year. For the past two years, approximately forty members of the Chinese Ministry of Health have been invited by the League of Nations to study specialized subjects in Europe, the United States, and Japan. Regarding construction matters, it is divided into education and engineering. Regarding education, a survey team recently came to China, consisting of Lange, Vandepop, and others. At the request of the Ministry of Education, the League of Nations also sent one professor of geography, one professor of geology, and one professor of English literature. The situation is also very active in engineering. Haas, Chairman of the League of Nations Transportation Committee, arrived in Shanghai today (yesterday) and will replace Dr. Lachman in his work on the Economic Committee after Dr. Lachman leaves China. Three technicians will also come to China in half a month. In addition, two other technicians will use their expertise to assist the Economic Committee and other relevant agencies. Their stay in China will be quite long. In short, the cooperation between the Chinese Economic Committee and the League of Nations is both close and active, which can be stated with certainty.

Hu Siyi Returns to China After Completing Studies in the United States

Hu Siyi, the second son of Mr. Hu Qibing, Director of Registration at Guanghua University, has studied in the United States for seven years and has received a Master of Business Administration degree from Syracuse University. He served as a teaching assistant at the university for one year and worked at the New York State Bank and the New York National Trust Bank, a well-known national bank, for two years each. At the same time, he was elected Vice President of the Chinese Economic Society of America and also studied economics and banking at the Graduate School of Economics at Columbia University. He has gained a great deal of knowledge and experience. He has now arrived in Shanghai and will make great contributions to the banking industry in China.

Two Important Telegrams from Various Road Business Associations

The Shanghai General Federation of Business Associations sent two telegrams to the Fourth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee yesterday, expressing its views on national defense and financial issues. The texts of the telegrams are as follows:

Please Hold Jinzhou Nanjing Central Party Headquarters Fourth Plenary Session First Central Committee

Gentlemen, since the violent enemy troops suddenly approached our Liaoning and Jilin on the evening of September 18, the proper practice of legitimate self-defense under international law has not been applied. We begged for help from the League of Nations, but the League of Nations was indifferent. We invoked the covenant, but the covenant was ineffective. We allowed Ma Zhanshan to fight alone in Heilongjiang Province with limited troops and isolated forces, and the provincial capital was lost. We allowed the troops stationed in Jinzhou to hold a corner without giving them support. Where are Zhang Xueliang's 200,000 border defense troops? The border defense commander does not go to the front lines and roams freely in Beiping. Since the completion of the Northern Expedition and the unification of the country, whenever there is an opinion or a minor disagreement within the country, soldiers with troops send letters and telegrams one after another, saying "armed request for service" or "ready to fight at any moment". Once a trouble starts, millions of troops gather quickly. This kind of coordination can shake mountains and shock the world. However, since the National Crisis on September 18, it has been three months. Apart from Zhang Fakui, who has not shed the spirit of a soldier defending the country, the other soldiers who have flaunted their power in the past two or three years not only do not rush to the aid and recover the lost territory, but the telegrams of "armed request for service" and "ready to fight at any moment" have not been seen once. Now, at the time of your meeting and when Jinzhou is in danger, you should immediately order the government to mobilize quickly, save Jinzhou to secure the whole country, and attack to recover the lost territory, to comfort the spirit of the late Premier in heaven and to live up to the people's hopes. We urgently send this telegram and respectfully ask for your adoption. Shanghai General Federation of Business Associations

Convene Economic Conference Nanjing Central Party Headquarters Fourth Plenary Session First Central Committee

Gentlemen, since the news reported that a certain Central Committee member advocated for the allocation of principal and interest on bonds, a panic broke out in Shanghai. The National Federation of Commerce and Industry declared in advance, and various public organizations sent letters and telegrams afterwards. Our association had previously assisted the Ministry of Finance in raising a huge amount of bonds, which led to a flood of inquiries and accusations from subscribers, which were impossible to handle. Fortunately, the news reported on the 25th that the proposal had been withdrawn by the original proposer, but no clear statement from the Central Government has been seen guaranteeing that the principal and interest on the bonds will continue to be paid without interruption. We believe that even if the item

Page 16

Proposal is withdrawn today, there is still concern that it may be revived in the future. In the humble opinion of our association, paying the principal and interest on the bonds according to the contract is a symbol of mutual trust between the people and the government. Otherwise, if the government loses its credibility with the people, the people will have no way to understand the government's position. In this time of frequent wars, famine, repeated foreign debts, and the violent Japanese invasion, it is difficult to conceal that the country's finances are unsustainable, even with Zhang Zongchang and Su Bao, it is difficult to hide the state. To resolve this crisis, the only way is to convene a national economic conference, gather representatives from the financial, industrial, and commercial sectors, and jointly devise solutions, determine policies, and, following the German precedent, empower it with full power of supervision and design. All resolutions should be implemented, so that everyone can work together with one heart to save the people from fire and water and to place the country on a solid foundation. Internal stability and external resistance will be matters of course. We send this telegram with utmost urgency. Shanghai General Federation of Business Associations.

Merger and Organization of Two General Labor Unions

Meeting to be Held Today at 2 PM

Address: Pharmaceutical Association, Zhaojiabang Road

Since the realization of peaceful reunification, mass movements in various regions have flourished like bamboo shoots after a spring rain, with vigorous momentum. The workers in this city, numbering 800,000, previously had a General Labor Union, but it was later ordered to be disbanded because the Labor Union Law stipulated by the Legislative Yuan did not include such an organization. Recently, feeling the trend of the times, workers throughout the city have been discussing the establishment of a General Labor Union. However, due to the urgency of time and insufficient prior communication, the strange event of two General Labor Unions being established simultaneously in Zhabei on the 20th of this month occurred. It has been learned that people in the labor sector generally feel pained by the lack of unity in the worker organization and the future of the labor movement. Therefore, Zhou Xuexiang, Yu Xianting, Weng Ruifu, and others have been mediating to the best of their ability. It is reported that both sides have expressed understanding and agreed to convene a discussion meeting at 2 PM today (the 27th) at the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union on Zhaojiabang Road in the South City, bringing together responsible personnel from the two General Labor Unions to discuss cooperation issues. Regarding the existing dual organization and the previously elected executive and supervisory committee members, they may be automatically canceled and a general meeting of representatives from the city's labor sector will be reconvened for re-election.

Scholarship Association Increases Essay Award Money

The Scholarship Association, organized by academic circles in this city, presented three essay topics for the first time the other day, as previously reported. It is now learned that Mr. Tang Jicang has specially donated 100 yuan in prize money for the third topic proposed by the association. For those who pass the third topic, the association will not only award the original amount of prize money, but also add the prize money donated by Mr. Tang. The content of the third topic is as follows: Economic severance with Japan is generally regarded as a key to saving the country. Among economic severances, boycotting Japanese goods is particularly important. Which Japanese goods can be replaced by domestic goods, and which can only be temporarily replaced by goods from other countries? How much do their uses and prices differ from Japanese goods? How can consumers avoid losses and permanently boycott Japanese goods? Furthermore, if raw materials for imitating foreign goods come from Japan, where should alternative raw materials be used? How much do their uses and prices differ from Japanese goods? Can they be manufactured domestically, and what would the manufacturing cost be? Please investigate in detail their categories, sales volume, value, function, and comparison with substitutes, as well as the cost of domestic manufacturing, and list them in two separate tables: (A) Commodities; (B) Raw materials for imitating foreign goods. Listing ten items in each table will be considered passing. The table should include the following items: (1) Name of Japanese goods; (2) Sales volume; (3) Price (indicate the unit); (4) Function; (5) What kind of substitute; (6) Comparison of the function of the substitute with Japanese goods; (7) Comparison of the price of the substitute with Japanese goods; (8) Difficulty of domestic manufacturing; (9) Estimated cost of domestic manufacturing; (10) Estimated price of domestically produced goods (indicate the unit). Add an explanation after the table. All details of the association's essay contest and award methods are detailed in the twelfth issue of the New Society semi-monthly magazine published at 142 Weihaiwei Road.

Minutes of the Shanghai County Executive Committee Meeting

The Shanghai County Party Department held its 35th Executive Committee meeting yesterday morning. The National Goods Review Publication to be Published

The National Goods Review publication has been in existence for seven years and has been well-received by people at home and abroad, with increasing sales. In this time of national crisis, the publication, under the slogan of resisting Japan and saving the country, has become even richer in content. In addition to publishing inscriptions and speeches from party and state figures full of revolutionary spirit, it also offers detailed analyses and insightful judgments on the inside story of the events in the Eastern Provinces. It also provides effective methods for the work of resisting Japan and saving the country, which can serve as a reference for all sectors. The other articles are full of tears and blood, providing readers with a deeply profound stimulation. It is now being bound and is scheduled to be published at the end of this month. Out-of-town mail orders will be sent upon receipt of three cents in postage.

The 6th and 7th issues of Business Monthly, published by the Business Monthly Society on Ximen Xunlan Road, Shanghai, is a "Special Issue on Japan." It is truly an essential publication for resolving the current domestic economic crisis and the issue of Japan. It is reported that the special issue is sold separately for 40 cents, and the annual subscription for twelve issues is still one yuan without any price increase.

The China Travel Service has published the first collection of books on the travel industry, "Capital Guide". Other information such as the schedules and prices of water, land, and air transportation, as well as Nanjing's streets and hotels, are listed in detail, making it an essential book for those traveling to the capital. It is essential to have this book for reference.

After Defiling Her, He Sold Her Body

The Youth Yu Kecheng Was Too Unconscionable

Pawnshop Uncovers Abduction Case During Redemption

Huang Bode, a local resident who works as a printing foreman, lives at No. 779 Jin Yuan Lane, Carter Road. Two years ago, he married Sheng Meida through a matchmaker. Sheng was 29 years old and quite beautiful. Since their marriage, the couple had been very harmonious. However, on the morning of the 14th of last month, Sheng went out to shop and never returned. Huang suspected that his wife had suddenly disappeared and became suspicious. He checked the suitcases and discovered that she had taken away dozens of silver dollars, a gold pin, and two pawn tickets. The pawn tickets were for two items of newly made camel wool and gabardine qipaos that had been pawned at Changfeng Pawnshop on Shanhaiguan Road. He reported the matter to the police station, requesting them to investigate, and also informed Changfeng Pawnshop that if anyone came to redeem the items, they should be detained. On the 20th of this month, a Cantonese youth named Yu Kecheng (only 19 years old, residing at No. 1654 Haining Road) came to the pawnshop to redeem the items with the tickets. Huang was secretly notified, who reported it to the Xinzha Police Station. The police dispatched detectives to arrest Yu at the pawnshop. A gold pin belonging to Sheng was found on Yu's person. Under questioning, Yu admitted to raping and selling Sheng Meida without denying it, but also stated that his accomplice, Chen Yinshi, was hiding at No. 265 Kaierzier Road in the French Concession. Chinese and Western detectives then worked together with detectives from the French Concession to bring Chen Yinshi back, along with a suspect named Qian Arong, and detained them separately. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, presented the case, submitted the gold pin as evidence, and stated that Sheng Meida, the abducted woman, had been sold to Hankou, requesting a postponement to send detectives to Hankou for investigation. Huang Bode, the plaintiff, also submitted a report, explaining the above situation. Yu Kecheng, the defendant, confessed that he had known Sheng for a short time and that he was unemployed. One day, he met Chen Yinshi in Yanziwo. After talking, on the seventh day of the tenth lunar month, he, Chen Yinshi, and Sheng Meida went to Hankou together on the Xiangyang ship and stayed at the home of his friend Yu Binqi at No. 73 Shencheng Lane, Jiaotong Road. Later, because his business was unsuccessful, Chen Yinshi found a way to sell Sheng. The total price was 320 yuan, of which he received 90 yuan, and the rest was taken by Chen. On the 12th of this month, he returned to Shanghai with Chen. The day before yesterday, he attempted to redeem the pawned items at Changfeng Pawnshop and was arrested. He confirmed that the gold pin was given to him by Sheng. Chen Yinshi stated that she had previously been punished by the French Concession for an abduction case. This time, because Yu was unemployed, she went to Hankou with Yu and Sheng and stayed at the Jiaotong Hotel for about a month. Yu's business was still unsuccessful, and the daily expenses were already substantial, and they owed a lot of travel expenses. Sheng voluntarily offered to help, so Chen Qinhuang introduced them, and she sold Sheng to No. 16 Lunhe Lane, Xingsheng Road (Chinese territory), Hankou to work as a prostitute under the alias Wang Eryuan. At that time, a promissory note was written for 320 yuan. After deducting the flag fees, the remaining amount was taken by Yu. Qian Arong had nothing to do with it. She came to Shanghai to prepare the money to redeem the clothes Sheng had pawned in order to redeem her. Qian Arong claimed that he had nothing to do with this matter. Judge Wu Tingqi verified the confessions and ordered Qian to provide a guarantor who could be summoned at any time, and to await investigation, as Sheng Meida had not yet been found. Yu Kecheng and Chen Yinshi were sent back to prison. The police were ordered to send detectives to Hankou to find Sheng Meida for further verification.

Ningbo Woman Sues Husband's Brother

For Holding onto Shared Property

Ye Hong, a woman from Zhenhai, Ningbo, found that after her husband, Ye Wende, passed away in the eleventh year of the Republic, he was still living in his former residence. Recently, she found that when her father-in-law, Ye Yufan, died, he left behind property worth about 200,000 yuan, which her husband's brother, Ye Yuande, was holding onto. He was in charge of Wende's share of the property but concealed it and refused to give it to her. Therefore, she came to Shanghai and hired lawyer Li Xinyang to sue Yuande in the Civil Court of the Special Court, demanding to divide the inheritance of her late father-in-law. Furthermore, she found that Ye Yufan had jointly purchased houses in Hongxingfang, Baoshan Road, Zhabei with Jiang Quanmao and Du Qiwen. On the day of the court hearing, Ye Yuande denied having this property. Ye Hong accused Ye Yuande of denying the existence of proven property, which constituted an act of encroachment on shared property, and filed a criminal complaint of embezzlement with the Special Court. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Shen Bingrong opened the Fifth Criminal Court to summon the defendant, Ye Yuande, who did not appear due to illness. His lawyer was appointed to represent him in court. First, Ye Hong claimed that after her best efforts, she found that Yufan also had 144 shares of the China Electric Company's stock, valued at 1,440 yuan, which the defendant had pawned at Renheng Money Shop on October 14 of this year. There were also 1,500 yuan of Qinhuangdao Liujiang Coal Mine stock, three shares of Ningshao Shipping Company stock, and stock in the Coal Industry Five Lines. This property was all purchased by her late father-in-law and was recently discovered by her, so it was not listed in the complaint. The defendant's lawyer then requested an adjournment, stating that the defendant was indeed ill and unable to appear in court, and requested a postponement, submitting the prescription as evidence. Subsequently, lawyer Li Xinyang briefly supplemented the plaintiff's statements. Judge Shen then adjourned the case for further hearing.

Hongyu Cloth Factory Robbery Case Solved

Ling Xichao, the district chief of the Second District of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, ordered an investigation into a robbery that occurred at the Hongyu Weaving Factory at No. 439 Zhaozhou Road on November 21 of this year. It is now learned that the case was solved by Chen Wentong, a detective in the district, on the 24th of this month, based on a tip. He secretly reported it to squad leader Cao Junda, who reported it to District Chief Ling. Detectives Chen Wentong, Qin Chengming, Ren Bin, Zhu Jinxiu, Wang Shuangxi, Wang Tinggen, and others were dispatched to secretly cooperate with the Second Precinct of the Sixth District and rushed to a house at No. 14 Hongqiao Road. They arrested Qu Jinyang, one of the robbers in the case, and interrogated him at the district headquarters. He also confessed that his accomplices were at the Yahui Building on Shangwen Road. Squad leader Cao then dispatched detectives to the location provided by the suspect. They arrested the robbers Shi Youming and Mao Fuqing (Shi Youming's teacher), who were suspected of being involved, and brought them all to the district headquarters. They were then subjected to interrogation by District Chief Ling. Shi Youming confessed to robbing property from the Hongyu Weaving Factory. He also confessed to robbing the Yixin Silk Weaving Factory at No. 17 Weiwu Road, Jumen Branch Road, on April 1, taking away banknotes, woolen cloth, men's and women's clothing, etc., worth about 500 to 600 yuan. However, he confessed that a pistol had been taken away by Shi's mistress and its whereabouts were unknown, so it could not be traced. After District Chief Ling ascertained the facts, the case involved robbery, so he should prepare a document and submit it to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning, along with the names, ages, and addresses of the robbers. Shi Youming, 27 years old, from Haimen, currently residing at No. 6 Dong'an Lane, Fangxie Road. Qu Jinyang, 27 years old, from Nantong, currently residing at No. 14 Hongqiao Road. Mao Fuqing, 42 years old, from Haimen, currently residing at No. 99 Daji Road.

Petty Thief Steals Small Silver Box

At noon yesterday, at the Yebiji Tea Shop near Wangjia Wharf in the South City, the shop's staff were having lunch when a naughty boy suddenly came in. Taking advantage of the shop's unpreparedness, he sneaked under the counter and grabbed a small silver box from the counter. He then climbed out of the counter and ran away. Fortunately, a shop assistant named Tang Shoujin from Sijing saw him and quickly gave chase. The boy saw someone chasing him and knew things were not going well, so he threw the stolen small silver box on the side of the road. Tang picked up the silver box and continued to chase, shouting loudly to catch the thief. When he reached the entrance of Wangjia Wharf Limei Road, Nan Shengwen, the police officer on duty at the second post there, heard the commotion and intercepted the boy. He took him to the First Precinct of the First District. During the preliminary interrogation by the precinct chief, Tang Qijin, 41 years old, stated the details of the incident and requested punishment. The boy confessed that his name was Zhou Tingrong, 14 years old, from Wenzhou, residing on Sangwei Street outside Xiaonanmen. He confessed to stealing the small silver box from the Yebiji Tea Shop. It was found that the boy was young and small, and often sneaked into shops to steal when people were not prepared. He had been arrested for such incidents dozens of times. This time, he dared to steal the small silver box from the tea shop and was caught on the spot. It was clear that he was incorrigible. He was ordered to prepare a document and submit it to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Opium Harms People One After Another

Due to Xu's Wrongful Accusation

A woman from Jiangyin named Xie Dajie lived with Jiang Yinsheng from Huangyan in her hometown. Xie's father had a severe opium addiction. Due to illness, he asked Xie Dajie to come to Shanghai to buy 27 taels of opium, which she hid in a rattan basket. Two months ago, she went to the North Railway Station to take a train back to her hometown. At the station, she met Jiang Yinsheng's wife, Xu, who was also returning home. Xie entrusted her luggage to Xu for safekeeping while she went to buy a train ticket. Unexpectedly, the police officer checking the luggage found the opium. Xu claimed that it belonged to Xie Dajie, but Xie had already fled, resulting in Xu being transferred to the local court and sentenced to six months in prison. She is currently still in jail. Later, Jiang Yinsheng negotiated with Xie's father, who died suddenly. Yesterday afternoon at 1:30, Jiang Yinsheng was walking across Fangbang Bridge outside Xiaobeimen when he met Xie Dajie. He immediately called the police officer Li Huixuan, who arrested her. According to the interrogation by Chief Xu, Xie Dajie admitted to the plaintiff's accusation of entrusting her to carry the opium. As the case had already been filed with the court, she was sentenced and sent to the local court for handling.

Luban Road: At 6:20 last night, two robbers suddenly came to the home of Xu Yongzuo at No. 3, Lane 157, Luban Road, French Concession. They showed a pistol and ordered everyone to remain silent. After ransacking the place, they took away clothes and silver dollars worth over 400 yuan. As they left, they fired a shot at the entrance to show their power, but no one was injured. Afterwards, the victim filed a loss report with the police station, requesting an investigation.

Kaierzier Road: Around 1:00 last night, two robbers broke into a hotel at No. 29, Kaierzier Road, Eight Immortals Bridge, French Concession. They each held a pistol and looted at will, searching for about twenty minutes before leaving with their loot. After a detailed investigation, the loss, including clothes and silver dollars, was about 300 yuan. Afterwards, the victim filed a report with the police station, requesting an investigation.

Minutes of the Anhui Provincial Association Standing Committee Meeting

The Anhui Provincial Association in Shanghai held its 15th Standing Committee meeting yesterday. Li Zhenya chaired the meeting. After the general secretary's report, the following resolutions were made: (1) To ratify the various aid cases that have already been handled. (2) Representatives of the Anhui Provincial All-Circles Pro-Chen Relief Province Assembly, Sun Jingxi, Xu Xiyong, and others, reported on Chen Tiaoyuan's disaster in Anhui, listing six major crimes and requesting support. Resolved: Telegrams will be sent to the Fourth Plenary Session, the National Government, and the Control Yuan requesting dismissal and strict punishment, and the matter will be handed over to the liaison office of the Association of Overseas Provincial Associations for handling. (3) Representatives from Fengtai, Liao Yuanqiao, Dingyuan, Fang Haiqiu, Shouxian, Wang Songzhai, and Xuyi, Fu Zhaogen, reported that Chen Tiaoyuan was ignoring the disaster victims and forcibly collecting the Weitian tax that had already been suspended. The people were unable to pay, and they requested assistance. Resolved: A telegram will be sent to the Central National Government, strictly ordering the Anhui Provincial Government to stop, and letters will be sent to the various leaders, informing them not to pay. (4) The Ying Shan County Government and various legal groups sent letters requesting assistance in the case of Hu Rengchu, a student from Shanghai who was arrested. Resolved: Copy the Songhu Garrison Headquarters' reply that Hu Rengchu had been sentenced to two years and six months in prison, and send a letter to the county's legal groups for verification. (5) The Huoqiu Provincial Association in Bengbu requested unanimous retention of Zheng Tingzhen's brigade to maintain local security. Resolved: A telegram will be sent to retain the brigade. (6) Wang Funong, Cheng Hanxing, and others from the Wuyuan Provincial Association reported that the Wuyuan county government was completely burned down by bandits. The Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces have sent troops to encircle and suppress them, but the Anhui Provincial Government has not yet replied. They requested assistance. Resolved: A telegram will be sent to the Central National Government requesting the dispatch of troops to clear the bandits. (7) Representatives from Fuyang and Fengtai counties, Xing Yuanxing and others, requested assistance because the provincial government had ordered the issuance of road construction public bonds, which they were unable to afford. Resolved: Reply to the counties that they should not pay, and hand the matter over to the liaison office for joint handling. (8) Soliciting members. Resolved: Continue to work hard to promote the solicitation of members. New-style certificates will be issued to those who have paid the fees and registered, and a New Year's gathering and worship ceremony will be held for all team leaders of the solicitation committee, all members of the disaster relief committee, and all directors, supervisors, and staff members of this organization. Active efforts will be made to advance the various association affairs.

Frozen Male Corpse in a Chicken Coop

Outside Wangjia Wharf on the South City Outer Road, there was a chicken coop. Yesterday, a male corpse was suddenly found inside. The man was about 40 years old and was wearing a black cotton-padded jacket and pants. There was a piece of torn cotton wool next to him. It is thought that he entered the coop to take shelter from the wind but still froze to death. The sixteenth district chief reported the incident to the local court for examination.

Reader's Letter

News of Mr. Liu Jisheng

(Advocating the use of Japanese goods to reward soldiers fighting against Japan)

Regarding Mr. Zhang Liyang and Mr. Li Shi's inquiries as published in your esteemed newspaper about how to handle the sealed Japanese goods, I, due to being on military campaign, was unable to read them, which I deeply regret. However, I greatly agree with Mr. Xing Li's proposal to use Japanese goods as military expenses against Japan, which is like fighting poison with poison. The Japanese education system always shows children how to seize Chinese land to obtain China's precious, beautiful, playable, and edible items, in order to induce their ambition to scheme against us. It cannot be said that this is not far-sighted. We should now take the most beautiful Japanese goods as rewards to encourage the soldiers fighting against Japan. Woolen and other fabrics should be used for military uniforms, and other valuable items should also be used for comfort purposes. It is absolutely forbidden to auction them off to obtain money for military expenses. Because if we auction them off, the mistake might cause our people to covet cheap prices and still buy Japanese goods (our slogan is not to buy Japanese goods!). If we wait until goods can be imported before paying money, then those who destroy their homes to help the country are not worthy of praise. We should bankrupt ourselves to save the country, and only then can we show this to our people.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The weather in the Yangtze River Basin and the Shandong coastal area is unstable with rain. Youth Corner

Hometown

— Huo Jin

Whenever anyone hears the word "hometown," they are bound to reminisce with lingering and quiet thoughts, fondly recalling the sweet and comfortable life of the past, especially thinking of the caring and warmth of their loving mother, the small, yet endless kindness. This makes those who are wanderers feel that this kind of love is infinitely great and unforgettable for a lifetime. Changing the way of thinking, feeling that the broad love of a loving mother cannot be enjoyed for a lifetime, one becomes gloomy and sad. Therefore, those who study thousands of miles away or seek a living far from home, if their white-haired, aging mother still exists, who wouldn't want to seize a spare moment to go home and enjoy the warm affection that flows from nature?

Recently, our Miss Jin, because she wanted to rush into the arms of her loving mother and receive her mother's comfort, took the opportunity of the school's few days of closure and gracefully returned home. Miss Yin also went to her hometown in Zhenjiang, where the provincial government is located. She goes there often. Several times a month, her beautiful figure can be found on the Nanjing-Shanghai train. As for myself, it's quite pitiful to say. I haven't seen my hometown, which is as beautiful as a painting, for three full years. At this time, seeing people going back one after another, how can I not be moved? Therefore, I also want to point my toes towards my hometown and step back.

However, my return this time is not to fall into the arms of my loving mother, to laugh heartily for a while, or to cry bitterly, to enjoy the influence of her love. No. Is it to appreciate the excellent scenery of my hometown, to wash away the accumulated filth in my mind, which has been buried in the hustle and bustle of Shanghai all day long? No, it's not for any of these reasons. The biggest motivation for my return is to go back to comfort my precious sister, Yu Mei, whom I have been separated from for three years and who is now groaning in bed with illness.

Alright, my hometown, the county named Longxi, has surprisingly appeared before my eyes. In my mind, the situations that I had lingered here three years ago, scene by scene, recurring thoughts, layers of past events, are all folding in my heart. Oh, at this time, is my mood sweet, bitter, sad, or happy? Awkward as I am, I still can't describe it with my pen.

From her expression, Yu Mei is still the Yu Mei from three years ago. Although she is already married, she still has a naive and innocent look. Although she is ill, her face still shows a pretty and lovely expression, without a hint of haggard and dejected morbidity. Her family members all say that she has lost weight, but according to my observation, she doesn't seem to be any thinner than she was when she was a child. This is probably because her body was a little fatter in the early days after her marriage.

Yu Mei's illness started after childbirth. Less than a month after giving birth, she suddenly fell ill. The illness was no small matter, but rather very serious. The old women in her family are all idol worshippers. They made a fuss over everything from drawing lots to asking for divination, to inviting witches to pray to the gods. On the other hand, they also sought medical treatment. By the time I went to her house, her illness had already subsided. However, a breast abscess had grown on her right breast. This was due to binding her chest in her childhood. Pus and blood were congealed on her breast, like a rotten peach. When she changed the plaster, she frowned, all anxious. How could she not frown when she peeled off the hard plaster from her already rotten skin, making her feel unbearable pain? Moreover, she had to insert seven or eight medicine threads into the rotten flesh, making people even more frightened to see it. At that time, I proposed that after changing the medicinal powder, she should no longer apply the plaster. It would be best to apply things like medicated cotton gauze and rubber plasters. This would reduce her pain. Who knew that in this rural area with inconvenient transportation, it was impossible to buy these things with money? Even in the only small hospital here, the number of these things was limited. Even if you paid a high price, you couldn't buy more. If I had known that she was in this kind of embarrassing situation, I would have bought some and brought them to her in Shanghai long ago. On this breast abscess, the areola that has not yet rotted seems to have become hardened. If you lightly touch it with your finger, she would simply scream in pain. Moreover, every day at dusk, the nipple would throb, making her even more uncomfortable.

Yu Mei's husband, Mr. Xue An, is a sincere young man. Although I only met him for the first time, I have been corresponding with him for more than a year. From his letters, I know that he is a very studious, warm-hearted, and promising young man. Although he was born into an old-fashioned gentry family, he doesn't have any of the characteristics of a playboy. His family runs a storefront and a large shop. Because he is the eldest son and there is a lack of able-bodied people in the family, he is required to take care of things in the shop, one thing at a time, three times seven equals twenty-one. Therefore, he did not have the opportunity to go out for further studies, but was instead married off early. However, in his spare time, he always diligently reads books and newspapers and whips himself on. Therefore, his knowledge and insights can be truly said to be outstanding among the young people in my hometown.

Since he is a descendant of the gentry, his family is undoubtedly a large family. In this large family, if something happens, it is easy to get help. Especially if someone gets sick, the experienced wives, related uncles, nephews, aunts, and cousins all have enthusiasm and carefully serve the sick, feeding them tea and soup, and talking to relieve their worries. This is very difficult to achieve in a simple small family, where everything must be done by servants. Every evening, after dinner, everyone is idle and gathers in the room where Yu Mei is resting, with grandmothers, aunts, grandmothers, girls, and young uncles, all gathered together, crying and laughing, how lively. Yu Mei, who is lying in bed and constantly groaning, will also talk and laugh when she is happy, and therefore forget the pain. However, sometimes when she gets tired, she impatiently closes her eyes and pretends to be asleep. Because she has taken a lot of medicine when she was sick and her body is weak, her ears are not very clear. But if there is a noisy sound around her, how can she not hear it and feel annoyed?

Although Yu Mei has become a mother, she is still a bit childish. Whenever she loudly complains about the pain in her breasts, I will tell her some stories. What she likes to hear the most are those fairy tales with supernatural and mysterious elements. When she concentrates and listens intently, she will even gesticulate with her hands and feet, completely forgetting all the pain in her body.

Furthermore, Yu Mei's crystallization of love is a girl who is less than two months old, with white skin, beautiful and lovely, her eyes shining brightly as she looks at people, without any fear of strangers. She eats the wet nurse's milk, but Yu Mei holds her in her arms and caresses her several times a day at least. Although Yu Mei's illness was caused by this child, she never hates her. Instead, she reveals the love of nature and applies it to this little treasure. Ah, the love between mother and child, how great it is.

Since Yu Mei became ill, she has not eaten any solid food at all. Every day she only sips a mouthful of porridge. When I went, it was just when her illness was gradually recovering. People who have recovered from a long illness are naturally very hungry. She felt that congee was not filling enough, so she clamored for rice. But her in-laws, because her stomach was weak after her illness, were afraid that she would not be able to digest it, so they still gave her porridge to eat. She then threw a childish tantrum, seemingly

Page 20

angrily saying, "A beggar, when begging for food from people, will surely get some rice after going to several houses. But I have begged you for rice for many days, and you still refuse to give me rice. Am I not even like a beggar?" This made everyone laugh. Later, with the doctor's permission, she was gradually given some rice to eat.

I stayed in Longxi for a week, and Yu Mei's illness slowly recovered. However, the thick blood flowing from her breast has not stopped. According to the doctor, "It is feared that it will not be possible to achieve the effect of closing the sore in a short period of time, but there will be no more troubles." She has suffered enough for the pain of this rotten sore in her breast. Alas, how pitiful.

This time, I discovered two pleasant things in my hometown that I hadn't seen for three years. First, the current district chief is our female compatriot, Shen Qingquan from Hangzhou. I once visited her. She is about thirty years old, speaks extraordinarily, and is a very capable person. Since she took office in March of this year, she has benefited the local area a lot, and the people have praised her endlessly. Everyone says, "She is much better than the corrupt district chief from before." Second, the education of local girls in middle school has now been established. In the past, it was a rural area with only a few primary schools and private schools for boys and girls. Now, there is a Ms. Xie Guanghua, a native of this village, who graduated from Shanghai's Shanghai University and has served in the education field for many years with excellent academic experience. Because she realized that education in her hometown was underdeveloped, she resolutely returned to Longxi to found a Zhicheng Primary School. The system includes primary and junior high school, but because the local customs are stubborn, boys and girls cannot study together, so it only accepts girls. Therefore, the general girls who have graduated from primary school can have the opportunity to receive secondary education. However, the customs of this township are still full of stubborn qualities, and the general girls who have graduated from primary school often have no intention of moving forward and are busy making wedding dresses instead of continuing their studies. Therefore, there are only a little over twenty students in the junior high school here, which cannot but be said to be a regret.

Two days before my return to Shanghai, one unforgettable thing was to go to the final resting place of my deceased parents to sweep the tomb. It is a piece of land with a small stream in front, mulberry and bamboo planted in the back, and scattered weeds in the middle, protruding and growing. In this piece of land with less than three years of history, sleep the sacred bodies of my strict and loving parents who abandoned me, a lonely and weak daughter. Their voices and smiles still linger in my memory. But at this time, even if I shed all my sad tears and shouted until my anxious throat was hoarse, how can I resurrect the dead and make the bones white and make the strict and loving ones who have returned to heaven come back to life so that I can listen to their loving voices again, kiss their kind and blessed faces again, throw myself into their arms again, and receive their comfort? My parents have passed away for several years, and I am still floating and sinking in this vast sea of humanity, lonely, helpless, desolate, and without appeal. Dear parents, if you know that your weak daughter is living such a lonely life, how sad would you be?

Page 21

Youth Corner

A Handkerchief

— Shan Jun

Old Wang, let's go watch the girls play basketball, how about it? No, who has so much free time to watch them play basketball? It's quite embarrassing, Hu said seemingly disdainfully. Don't say that, the red and green, the swaying, it's really quite interesting. Besides, hey, Little Sister is also playing.

Really? Hu seemed to be moved.

Who would lie to you?

Let's go, already expressed the greatest and final determination.

And so a large group of people, in a mighty manner, headed straight for the basketball court.

At this time, on the basketball court, only a mess of red pants and green clothes could be seen, with the sound of warblers and swallows scattering in all directions. Especially in the minds of every male classmate that was scattered in all directions, was naturally that immature person who we usually called Little Sister Cenzi. Now, the three words "Little Sister" seem to have succeeded in becoming her specialized term in our school. This, in the minds of our two honest men, Wang and Hu, could of course not be an exception. Little Sister, Little Sister, oh!

Hey, Old Wang, look, Little Sister dropped a handkerchief. Go quickly and pick it up. Isn't this the beginning of a contact? A once-in-a-lifetime opportunity, oh. Don't let someone else snatch it away. Old Wang!

No point. I don't want to have this kind of opportunity. I think, don't pretend to be upright in front of me like this again. Honestly, you should hurry up and pick it up and return it to her. You know that in this kind of situation, there's no use in being polite. Otherwise, it will be someone else's opportunity. Wang's words seemed to have some thorns in them.

What does it matter? In this socially open society, you say, I picked up a handkerchief for her, would anyone still say that I have other ambitions? That's really too vulgar.

Of course, who can say that? That's really too out of touch with the times, a bastard who deserves a slap in the face. Hey, go pick it up quickly. Look, this handkerchief has been trampled by their ruthless shoes into something unrecognizable. This should be such a pity.

Oh, is that so? Alas, that's really a pity. I must pick it up and return it to her. Otherwise, that's really too bad. God, give me some courage! Hu said, and it seemed that God had really given him a lot of courage. He moved his steps very spiritedly, but after taking only a few steps, he hurriedly came back with a face that had turned as red as a pig's liver.

Hey, Old Hu, what's wrong? Why did you take a few steps and shrink back?

I'm very afraid that the classmates will see it and shout. That wouldn't be good. I think it would be better to pick it up after everyone has left. What do you think?

Hehe…

What are you sneering at? Are you daring to ridicule me for not having the ability? Go, don't even talk about it. I'll definitely pick it up for you to see! Hu seemed to be enraged by Old Wang's great insult. And so he had to show Old Wang that he really had the determination and courage.

Who said you don't have the ability? But you said you were going to pick it up a long time ago, going to pick it up, but, until now, almost half an hour has passed, and I only hear you say "I must pick it up," "I must pick it up." That's enough for someone to have "ability"!

Okay, you wait and see!

Before long, the sky was gradually darkening. The red and green figures also slipped into the room one by one. The idlers naturally also dragged a satisfied laughter away. This was the time when our upright honest man, Hu, bravely began his work. But how long did it take, a second later…

Ah, run quickly, Old Wang! The handkerchief…although I picked it up, but…but my heart is…is…is in a panic and trembling!

And so, in the pale twilight, two black shadows sped away like lightning, quite like a thief encountering a watchman.
